### [36] [Dynamic Rollout Editing for Reducing Overthinking in RL-Trained Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17890)
*Zihao Wei,Wenjie Shi,Liang Pang,Jingcheng Deng,Shicheng Xu,Shasha Guo,Zenghao Duan,Jiahao Liu,Jingang Wang,Huawei Shen,Xueqi Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型在长链条推理中得出结论后仍继续无效思考的“过度思考”问题，研究者提出了一种动态回放编辑（DRE）训练干预方法，通过优化强化学习的信用分配，显著改善了模型的输出效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型在进行长链条思维（CoT）推理时，即使已经得出正确答案，仍倾向于继续生成冗余内容。这种现象被定义为“过度思考”。现有基于GRPO的强化学习无法有效区分得出结论的有效前缀与后续的冗余过程，导致模型在训练中不断强化这种低效行为。

Method: 作者提出了一种称为“动态回放编辑”（Dynamic Rollout Editing, DRE）的方法。该方法在强化学习训练过程中，识别出那些在得出正确答案后继续无效推理的路径，通过保留正确的推理前缀并剪裁后续冗余思考，将编辑后的路径与原始路径在同一个强化学习组中进行比较，从而降低模型生成不必要思考内容的倾向。

Result: 实验结果表明，DRE方法能够有效减少模型在得出答案后的“过度思考”行为，在维持任务准确率的同时，提升了模型推理输出的效率和简洁性。

Conclusion: 动态回放编辑（DRE）是一种有效的训练时干预手段，能够通过弱化不必要的思考过程的奖励信号，有效缓解大模型在强化学习后的“过度思考”问题，从而提升模型推理的效率和简洁性。

Abstract: Long-form chain-of-thought reasoning can improve LLM performance on complex tasks, but models often continue generating unnecessary reasoning after a correct answer has emerged. We refer to this behavior as overthinking. We study this phenomenon from the perspective of GRPO-style reinforcement learning (RL) post-training, framing it as a training-time credit-assignment problem rather than merely a decoding-time stopping problem. In rollouts sampled at the onset of GRPO training, we observe that successful trajectories can exhibit a slightly higher degree of overthinking than unsuccessful trajectories for the same prompts. This early imbalance provides a starting point for an undesirable feedback loop: because GRPO assigns sequence-level credit, it cannot distinguish the solution-reaching prefix from the unnecessary continuation that lengthens a successful trajectory. Both receive positive update signal, allowing the initial imbalance to grow into more severe overthinking during training. To address this issue, we introduce Dynamic Rollout Editing (DRE), a training-time intervention for successful trajectories that continue thinking after answer emergence. DRE preserves the accepted verified prefix, edits the remaining thinking, and prefers the edited trajectory within the same RL group, weakening the preference signal for unnecessary thinking without penalizing the reasoning needed to reach the answer. Experiments across diverse tasks show the effectiveness of DRE.

</details>


### [37] [ChLogic: Evaluating Robustness of Logical Reasoning in Chinese Expressions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17905)
*Peixian Zhou,Yuxu Chen,Chaorui Zhang,Wei Han,Bo Bai,Xueyan Niu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为 ChLogic 的英中对齐逻辑推理基准，发现大型语言模型在跨语言逻辑推理中存在显著且不一致的性能表现，揭示了语言表层特征与翻译对多语言推理能力的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大模型在英文标准化逻辑推理基准上表现出色，但其推理能力在跨语言（尤其是中文）场景下的稳健性尚不明确。研究旨在探究模型是否能在逻辑结构一致的前提下，在不同语言表层表达中保持推理的一致性。

Method: 构建了一个名为 ChLogic 的英中对齐基准测试集。该基准包含三个子集：基于通用命题的“通用对齐集”、基于复杂问题的“困难对齐集”以及涵盖中文特定语言现象的“仅中文集”。研究通过对比模型在英文原文与五种不同中文表达下的推理表现，并测试回译（back-translation）的效果来分析模型性能。

Result: 实验发现，Qwen3、Ministral 和 GLM 等模型在英中之间存在持续的性能差距。将中文回译为英文通常能提升通用对齐集的表现，但在处理复杂问题时效果不一，部分模型（如 Qwen3-32B 和 GLM-5.1）在回译后表现反而下降。

Conclusion: 研究表明，大型语言模型的逻辑推理能力在多语言环境下存在显著差异。中文表层表达、翻译伪影以及模型特定的行为共同影响了跨语言的推理表现。ChLogic 为评估多语言逻辑推理的稳健性提供了一个重要的压力测试工具。

Abstract: Large language models perform increasingly well on standardized logical reasoning benchmarks, but whether this ability remains robust beyond English is unclear. We introduce ChLogic, an English--Chinese aligned benchmark that tests whether models preserve logical reasoning performance when the same latent logical structure is expressed in English and diverse Chinese surface realizations. Built from formal logical templates, the benchmark contains three data sets: (i) the General aligned set, derived from 60 General Propositions across nine template families; (ii) the Difficult aligned set, derived from 40 Difficult Problems; and (iii) the Chinese-only set, covering 15 language-specific phenomenon types. Each aligned item pairs one English reference expression with five Chinese realizations. Experiments on Qwen3, Ministral, and GLM models reveal a persistent English--Chinese performance gap. Back-translation from standard Chinese into English often improves performance on the General aligned set, but produces mixed effects on the Difficult aligned set, where Qwen3-32B and GLM-5.1 perform worse after translation. These results indicate that Chinese surface realization, translation artifacts, and model-specific behavior jointly affect multilingual logical reasoning. Overall, ChLogic provides a useful stress test for the robustness of multilingual reasoning.

</details>


### [38] [Learning task-specific subspaces via interventional post-training of speech foundation models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17967)
*Jack Cox,Jon Barker*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于干预对比学习的语音表征解耦方法，成功将预训练语音模型中纠缠的信息分离为独立的内容和说话人子空间，显著提升了下游任务（如说话人验证）的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练的语音基础模型产生的表征通常包含多种语音信息，且以分布式方式纠缠在一起。然而，下游任务往往只需要其中特定的信息（如仅需内容或仅需说话人特征）。现有的模型难以直接获取这些解耦的表征，限制了其在特定任务中的表现和可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种基于干预对比学习（Interventional Contrastive Learning）的后训练优化方法。利用标注好的干预数据集和多部分对比损失函数（Multi-part Contrastive Loss），将原始语音模型中纠缠的表征空间映射并分离为相互独立的内容子空间和说话人子空间。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在说话人验证和关键词检测任务中表现优异，显著提升了模型在域外（Out-of-Domain）说话人验证任务中的性能，并证实了说话人信息与内容信息在学习到的子空间中得到了有效分离。

Conclusion: 通过干预对比学习，研究成功地将语音基础模型中纠缠的表征解耦为独立的说话人子空间和内容子空间，不仅提高了下游任务的性能，还增强了模型在处理未见数据时的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Speech foundation models, pre-trained on large corpora of unlabelled speech data, produce general-purpose representations which are useful across tasks. However, these representations encode information about salient speech variables in a distributed manner, while downstream speech tasks rely on only some of this variability. In this work, we propose a post-training refinement approach using interventional contrastive learning. By leveraging an interventional dataset and multi-part contrastive loss, we learn a transformation from the entangled representation space of speech foundation models into separate content and speaker subspaces. We evaluate the learnt representations on speaker verification and keyword spotting tasks, showing improved out-of-domain speaker verification performance and evidence that speaker and content information are separated across the learned subspaces.

</details>


### [39] [Fine-tuning LLMs for Passive Depression Severity Estimation from AI Mental Health Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17973)
*Olivier Tieleman,Ziyi Zhu,Ting Su,Samuel J. Bell,Thomas D. Hull,Caitlin A. Stamatis*

### [40] [VoidPadding: Let [VOID] Handle Padding in Masked Diffusion Language Models so that [EOS] Can Focus on Semantic Termination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17999)
*Chunyu Liu,Zhengyang Fan,Kaisen Yang,Alex Lamb*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决掩码语言模型（MDLM）中[EOS]标记既作终止符又作填充符导致的溢出问题，本文提出了VoidPadding方法，通过引入[VOID]标记实现角色解耦，显著提升了模型性能并降低了推理开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的MDLM在指令微调中沿用了自回归模型的习惯，将[EOS]标记同时用作语义终止符和填充符。这种双重角色是导致在大块解码（large-block decoding）过程中出现[EOS]溢出的根本原因。

Method: 提出了VoidPadding方法：引入特殊的[VOID]标记专门用于填充，将[EOS]标记保留仅用于语义终止。在推理过程中，利用[EOS]信号实现提前终止，利用[VOID]信号引导响应画布的自适应扩展。

Result: 在Dream-7B-Instruct模型上的测试表明，VoidPadding在数学推理和代码生成基准测试中，平均分比原始模型提高17.84分，比RainbowPadding提高6.95分，同时将解码所需的函数评估次数（NFE）平均降低了55.7%。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入VoidPadding机制，成功解耦了掩码语言模型（MDLM）中终止符和填充符的双重角色，有效缓解了EOS溢出问题，提升了生成质量并显著降低了推理成本。

Abstract: MDLMs generate text by denoising a preallocated masked response canvas, making response-length modeling central to instruction tuning. Existing MDLMs often inherit the autoregressive convention of using repeated \texttt{[EOS]} tokens for padding during instruction tuning, giving \texttt{[EOS]} a dual role as both a semantic terminator and a padding token. We show that this dual role is a root cause of \texttt{[EOS]} overflow under large-block decoding. To decouple these roles, we propose VoidPadding, which introduces \texttt{[VOID]} for padding and reserves \texttt{[EOS]} for termination. During inference, the learned \texttt{[EOS]} signal enables early stopping, while the learned \texttt{[VOID]} signal guides adaptive response canvas expansion. On Dream-7B-Instruct, VoidPadding improves the block-size-averaged four-task mean across mathematical reasoning and code generation benchmarks by \(+17.84\) points over the original model and \(+6.95\) points over RainbowPadding, while reducing decoding NFE by 55.7\% on average. Code is available at https://github.com/Haru-LCY/VoidPadding.

Abstract: Cross-lingual transfer in multilingual NLP has been widely explored in supervised fine-tuning contexts, where factors like data availability and linguistic similarity largely determine transfer quality. As the field shifts toward few-shot In-Context Learning (ICL), it is often presumed that insights from fine-tuning carry over unchanged. Yet this assumption has not been rigorously evaluated, leaving open the question of how to choose source languages for cross-lingual ICL. We conduct a broad empirical study of cross-lingual transfer in ICL spanning seven tasks, six models, and a typologically diverse set of languages. We further analyze language confusion, a key obstacle for generative tasks in cross-lingual ICL. Our results show that conventional fine-tuning-based expectations do not consistently apply in the ICL regime and point to alternative heuristics for selecting source languages effectively.

### [42] [Compositional Skill Routing for LLM Agents: Decompose, Retrieve, and Compose](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18051)
*Xueping Gao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SkillWeaver是一个处理复杂任务分解与技能组合的框架，通过引入迭代式技能感知分解（SAD）机制，解决了任务分解与现有技能库不匹配的核心瓶颈，有效提升了多技能协同执行的准确性和效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型代理主要侧重于单技能选择，无法应对需要多技能协作的复杂任务。针对技能组合路由问题（Compositional Skill Routing），现有方法缺乏有效的任务分解机制，导致任务分解与可用技能库不匹配，限制了执行效果。

Method: 提出SkillWeaver框架：1. 使用LLM进行任务分解；2. 结合FAISS索引的双编码器进行技能检索；3. 构建依赖感知的DAG（有向无环图）规划器。此外，提出了迭代式技能感知分解（SAD），通过检索增强反馈回路来对齐任务分解与现有技能库。

Conclusion: SkillWeaver通过迭代式技能感知分解（SAD）有效解决了复杂任务中的技能组合路由问题，证明了任务分解的粒度对技能检索和执行成功率具有决定性影响，同时也大幅提升了系统在资源利用和泛化方面的效率。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly rely on external skills -- reusable tool specifications -- but real-world tasks often require composing multiple skills, not just selecting one. We formalize this as the Compositional Skill Routing problem: given a complex user query and a large skill library, decompose the query into atomic sub-tasks, retrieve the appropriate skill for each sub-task, and compose an executable plan. We present SkillWeaver, a decompose-retrieve-compose framework combining an LLM task decomposer, a bi-encoder skill retriever with FAISS indexing, and a dependency-aware DAG planner. To support evaluation, we introduce CompSkillBench, a benchmark of 300 compositional queries over 2,209 real MCP server skills spanning 24 functional categories, sourced from the public MCP ecosystem. Our experiments reveal that task decomposition quality is the primary bottleneck: standard LLM decomposition reaches only 34.2% category recall at the step level. To address this, we propose Iterative Skill-Aware Decomposition (SAD), a retrieval-augmented feedback loop that iteratively aligns decomposition with available skills. SAD improves decomposition accuracy from 51.0% to 67.7% (+32.7%, Wilcoxon p < 10^-6) in a single iteration; DA-conditioned analysis confirms that correct granularity is the prerequisite for effective retrieval (CatR@1 rises from 34% to 41% when DA=1). SkillWeaver reduces context window consumption by over 99%, and transfer experiments confirm generalization (+35.6% relative DA gain even when target categories are absent from the retrieval pool).

### [43] [ConSA: Controllable Sparsity in Hybrid Attention via Learnable Allocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18056)
*Yao Chen,Yinqi Yang,Junyuan Shang,Xiangzhao Hao,Simeng Zhang,Yilong Chen,Tingwen Liu,Shuohuan Wang,Dianhai Yu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ConSA是一种利用L0正则化自动学习大模型中FA与SWA最优分配策略的框架，实现了在用户指定稀疏度下的高效推理优化，并揭示了模型注意力机制的非均匀分布特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结合全注意力（FA）和滑动窗口注意力（SWA）的混合架构多依赖于人工设计的规则，缺乏对注意力机制底层行为的深入分析与最优分配机制，导致推理效率提升有限。

Method: 提出了一种名为ConSA（Controllable Sparsity in Hybrid Attention）的框架，利用L0正则化技术学习每个注意力单元的FA/SWA分配二进制掩码，并通过增广拉格朗日乘子法（Augmented Lagrangian）在层级或KV头级强制执行预设的稀疏度约束。

Result: 在0.6B和1.7B规模的LLM上验证表明，ConSA学习到的分配方案优于人工规则基准。研究发现，KV头级别的分配方案表现更佳，且模型表现出将FA集中在中间层、SWA置于底层的固有行为模式。

Conclusion: ConSA揭示了LLM内部存在一种非均匀的注意力行为模式：模型倾向于在底层使用滑动窗口注意力（SWA），而在中间层集中使用全注意力（FA）。这种学习到的稀疏化模式优于传统的人工启发式规则，为高效大模型推理提供了一种系统化且可控的优化路径。

Abstract: Hybrid architectures combining full attention (FA) and sliding-window attention (SWA) are a promising paradigm for efficient LLM inference. However, existing methods typically rely on hand-crafted rules or simple post-hoc heuristics for FA/SWA allocation and offer limited analysis of the attention behaviors underlying these designs. We propose Controllable Sparsity in Hybrid Attention (ConSA), a framework that learns optimal FA/SWA assignment under a user-specified sparsity target. ConSA employs L0 regularization to learn binary masks selecting between FA and SWA for each attention unit, while an augmented Lagrangian constraint enforces the target sparsity at either layer or KV-head granularity. We evaluate ConSA on two LLMs at the 0.6B and 1.7B scales. Learned allocations consistently outperform rule-based baselines, with KV-head-wise allocation yielding clear gains over layer-wise allocation. The learned patterns place SWA in the bottom layers and concentrate FA into contiguous middle-layer blocks, diverging from evenly interleaved patterns in rule-based methods. This structure persists across model scales, sparsity levels, and allocation granularities, revealing a fine-grained spectrum of intrinsic attention behaviors that underlies the learned allocation.

Method: 研究者基于WildChat数据集中的320万条真实用户对话，筛选出14,727条S&P相关提示词。通过对其中450条进行主题分析以刻画用户需求，并专门构建了270条寻求建议的提示词，通过对每条提示词进行10次重复查询，评估了商业与开源大模型在回答质量及响应一致性方面的表现。

Conclusion: 尽管商业大模型在处理数字安全与隐私（S&P）问题上表现优于开源模型，但即便在高质量响应中也存在显著的一致性问题。这种响应的不确定性可能导致用户困惑甚至产生误导，强调了在安全敏感领域对LLM输出进行进一步校准和稳定化的必要性。

To the best of our knowledge, no prior study has collected or analyzed the S&P questions users ask LLMs; prior research on LLM response quality relied on expert-authored S&P misconceptions or FAQs rather than user queries. Drawing from WildChat, a dataset of 3.2M user-LLM conversations collected in the wild, our study identifies 14,727 S&P prompts and categorizes them into nine categories covering a wide range of S&P topics. From the S&P prompts, we sampled 450 and performed a thematic analysis to characterize the S&P questions users ask LLMs. Separate from the thematic analysis, we curated 270 advice-seeking S&P prompts, where users ask for recommendations, guidance, or specific S&P information. We measured LLM response quality and consistency when posing the prompt to LLMs 10 times. We found that commercial LLMs outperform open-weight models (GPT 5.5 provided "good enough" responses on 98% of prompts; Llama 4 on 47%). However, among prompts that received high-quality responses on average, commercial models sometimes produce contradictory responses across runs, risking confusing or misleading users.

### [45] [Unintended Effects of Geographic Conditioning in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18124)
*Naz Col,David M. Chan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了对话式AI中存在的“位置泄露”问题：模型即便接收中性指令，也会因用户元数据（甚至只是元数据框架）的干扰而产生强烈的地域偏见，这种偏见在顶级模型中依然普遍且严重。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代对话式AI系统常利用用户元数据来实现个性化响应，但这种隐藏的上下文往往会导致意想不到的地域偏见。研究者旨在量化并深入探究这种“位置泄露”现象及其产生的机理，以揭示AI模型在处理地理信息时的偏见程度。

Method: 研究人员通过在创意写作和开放式问答任务中，向处于前沿水平的LLM（如Llama 3.1, Qwen3, Claude Sonnet）输入地理位置元数据，并对比中性提示词下的输出差异，评估模型的地理位置泄露（location leakage）现象。此外，研究还引入了“Unknown”占位符实验，以验证用户配置文件框架本身的诱导作用。

Result: 实验显示，当模型接触到地理位置元数据时，会系统性地偏向生成特定地区的回答。地理位置泄露现象极为严重，在某些模型中激增幅度高达793倍。此外，研究发现，即便将位置信息替换为“Unknown”占位符，泄露率仍比基准线高出72倍，证实了用户画像框架本身即可作为一种生成式的条件信号，诱导模型产生地域偏差。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现代大型语言模型（LLM）不仅会受到地理位置元数据的直接引导产生地域偏见，还存在一种“结构性条件反射”效应——即仅通过用户配置文件的框架本身（即便内容为空或设为“未知”），也会诱发显著的地域偏差。这种隐性偏见揭示了模型对用户上下文上下文的过度依赖，对AI系统的公平性和中立性提出了挑战。

Abstract: Modern conversational AI systems frequently rely on user metadata to localize responses, yet the unintended regional biases introduced by this hidden context remain poorly understood. In this work, we evaluate location leakage: the phenomenon where a model generates geographic references despite receiving a geographically neutral user prompt. Across both creative writing and open-ended Q&A prompts, even state-of-the-art LLMs systematically favor region-specific outputs when exposed to location metadata, with leakage spiking by up to 793 times above baseline (e.g., from 0.04% to 31.7% for Llama 3.1-8B, and 21.3% and 8.8% for Qwen3-8B and Claude Sonnet 4.6, respectively). Our analysis further shows a novel structural conditioning effect: replacing the injected location with the placeholder "Unknown" still elevates leakage by up to 72 times above baseline, demonstrating that the user profile frame itself, independent of any geographic content, acts as a generative conditioning signal.

### [46] [Learning from the Self-future: On-policy Self-distillation for dLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18195)
*Yifu Luo,Zeyu Chen,Haoyu Wang,Xinhao Hu,Yuxuan Zhang,Zhizhou Sha,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: d-OPSD 是首个专为扩散大语言模型设计的自蒸馏框架，通过引入后置条件和步级监督，有效解决了现有方法与扩散生成机制的冲突，显著提升了模型的推理性能和训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 OPSD 方法主要针对自回归模型设计，依赖从左到右的前缀条件和 token 级监督，这与扩散式大语言模型（dLLMs）任意顺序生成的特性存在本质冲突，限制了其在 dLLMs 后训练中的应用。

Method: 1. 后置条件重构（Suffix Conditioning）：利用模型自生成的回答作为后缀条件，而非依赖特权前缀，使模型能够学习“自我未来经验”；2. 步级监督（Step-level Supervision）：将监督粒度从传统的 token 级调整为扩散模型的去噪步级，从而与 dLLMs 的迭代生成过程对齐。

Result: 在四个推理基准测试中，d-OPSD 的表现始终优于 RLVR 和 SFT 基线，且训练效率极高，所需的优化步数仅为 RLVR 的 10% 左右。

Conclusion: d-OPSD 成功将策略内自蒸馏（OPSD）范式引入扩散式大语言模型（dLLMs），证明了通过后置条件采样和步级监督，无需依赖外部奖励模型即可显著提升 dLLMs 的推理能力，且具有极高的训练效率。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has proven effective for post-training large language models (LLMs), yet its application to diffusion LLMs (dLLMs) remains unexplored. Existing OPSD methods are inherently autoregressive-centric. They inject privileged information via left-to-right prefix conditioning with token-level divergence supervision, a design that fundamentally conflicts with the arbitraryorder generation of dLLMs. We introduce d-OPSD, the first OPSD framework tailored for dLLMs. Our approach makes two core contributions. First, we reframe self-teacher construction by using self-generated answers as suffix conditioning, enabling the student model to learn from "self future-experience" rather than privileged prefixes. Second, we shift supervision from token-level to step-level, aligning training with the iterative denoising process of dLLMs. Experiments across four reasoning benchmarks show that d-OPSD consistently outperforms RLVR and SFT baselines with superior sample efficiency, requiring only around 10% of the optimization steps by RLVR and opening a promising pathway for dLLM posttraining. The code is available at https://github.com/xingzhejun/d-OPSD.

</details>


### [47] [RubricsTree: Scalable and Evolving Open-Ended Evaluation of Personal Health Agents across Health Memory and Medical Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18203)
*Weizhi Zhang,Zechen Li,Hamid Palangi,Ben Graef,A. Ali Heydari,Simon A. Lee,Salman Rahman,Ray Luo,Zeinab Esmaeilpour,Erik Schenck,Chloe Zhang,Yamin Li,Menglian Zhou,Philip S. Yu,Daniel McDuff,Lindsey Sunden,Mark Malhotra,Shwetak Patel,Ahmed A. Metwally*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为解决个人健康 AI 的评估瓶颈，本文提出了 RubricsTree，这是一个基于专家构建的层级分类准则框架，通过自适应路由实现高效率、高精度的自动化临床评估，显著提升了医疗大模型的性能表现。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出 RubricsTree 框架，利用包含超过 100 个原子化、临床可验证布尔准则的专家对齐层级分类体系。通过人机协作协议和经验丰富的医师团队，从 4,000 条真实用户查询中迭代构建准则；采用上下文感知自适应路由器，根据查询内容激活相关准则子集，实现高吞吐量与专家对齐的高质量评估。

Result: 实验证明，RubricsTree 在专家对齐度上显著优于现有的大规模评估基线；能可靠地识别并惩罚语境退化的回答；且将其作为结构化指令、文本反馈或训练奖励应用于 Gemini、GPT 和 Qwen 等模型时，在 HealthBench 上实现了高达约 66% 的性能提升。

Conclusion: RubricsTree 提供了一种可扩展、可审计且持续演进的评估基础设施，有效解决了个人健康 AI 在临床部署中的评估瓶颈，为提升医疗模型性能和安全性奠定了基础。

Abstract: The LLM-empowered personal health agents with user health (sensor) metrics have offered a promising pathway to alleviate global disparities in healthcare access. However, large-scale clinical deployment remains constrained by an open-ended evaluation bottleneck: physician annotation is reliable but costly and unscalable, while LLM-as-a-judge evaluators are scalable but subjective, inconsistent, and sometimes clinically misaligned. We introduce RubricsTree, a scalable evaluation framework with an expert-aligned hierarchical taxonomy of over 100 atomic, clinically-verifiable Boolean rubrics, evolving from the insights of 4,000 real user queries through an iterative human-in-the-loop curation protocol with an expertise panel led by an experienced physician. A context-aware adaptive router activates only the relevant auto-weighted rubric subset per query, providing the throughput needed for scalable evaluation with expert-aligned quality. Through a systematic meta-evaluation, we show that RubricsTree (i) substantially exceeds a strong large-scale evaluation baseline in expert alignment on challenging open-ended queries; (ii) reliably penalizes contextually degraded responses; and (iii) when used as structured instructions, text feedback, or training rewards for performance optimization, yields up to ~66% relative gains on HealthBench for Gemini, GPT, and Qwen model families. RubricsTree thus provides a scalable, auditable, and evolving evaluation infrastructure required for the continuous optimization of product-level personal healthcare AI.

Abstract: This paper presents a robust methodology for the systematic digitization and encoding of the Al-Mawrid Arabic-English dictionary, transforming it from a legacy print resource into a standardized computational lexicon. The methodology is grounded in an empirical analysis of the dictionary's lexical knowledge density. Drawing on a representative sample (the letter Ayn, comprising 4.6% of the total volume), the study provides scientific weight to the encoding process, demonstrating a structural parsing accuracy of 91%. Quantitative evaluation of the information extraction rules reveals high performance, with 85% precision and 98% recall for synonyms, and 88% precision for other morpho-semantic features. Beyond technical description, the paper provides a critical comparison with existing Arabic lexical resources and discusses the limitations of TEI Lex-0 when modelling specific Arabic phenomena, such as implicit "open set" semantic relations and scattered morphological cues. Furthermore, the study explores the potential for Linguistic Linked Open Data (LLOD) integration by establishing a scalable prefix-based referencing system that facilitates the resource's inclusion in the semantic web. The result is an interoperable, machine-tractable resource that provides a reproducible workflow for the retro-digitization of complex legacy bilingual lexicons within the Arabic NLP and Digital Humanities communities.

### [49] [Zone of Proximal Policy Optimization: Teacher in Prompts, Not Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18216)
*Byung-Kwan Lee,Ximing Lu,Shizhe Diao,Minki Kang,Saurav Muralidharan,Karan Sapra,Andrew Tao,Pavlo Molchanov,Yejin Choi,Yu-Chiang Frank Wang,Ryo Hachiuma*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出ZPPO算法，通过将教师反馈转化为提示词而非梯度干预，解决了小模型在强化学习训练中的性能瓶颈与策略漂移问题，显著提升了小模型的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 知识蒸馏在小参数模型中存在过拟合教师尖锐特征的问题，而现有的强化学习方法在面对模型无法产生有效输出的难题时，强制注入教师反馈会破坏在线策略假设并导致策略漂移。

Method: 提出了“近端近侧策略优化”（ZPPO），通过构建“二进制候选提示（BCQ）”和“负面候选提示（NCQ）”将教师知识融入提示中，并引入“提示重放缓冲区”机制，让模型在被定义的“近侧发展区间”内反复学习难点样本，直到掌握为止。

Result: 在Qwen3.5系列模型（0.8B-9B）与27B教师模型的实验中，ZPPO在31个多模态基准测试上全面优于离线/在线蒸馏及GRPO方法，且模型规模越小，提升幅度越显著。

Conclusion: ZPPO通过将教师的指导置于提示工程（Prompting）而非策略梯度中，有效解决了强化学习中因教师干预导致的策略漂移问题，证明了在小参数规模模型上实现高效知识迁移的可行性。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation transfers a teacher's competence to a small student but is brittle in the small-student regime: forcing the student to imitate logits from a much larger teacher concentrates it on the teacher's sharpest modes, hurting generalization on benchmark families beyond the training corpus. Reinforcement learning (RL) avoids logit imitation by training on the student's own rollouts. However, on questions where every rollout fails-yielding zero advantage and being silently discarded-injecting a stronger teacher's response into the policy gradient breaks the on-policy assumption and induces drift. We introduce Zone of Proximal Policy Optimization (ZPPO), inspired by Vygotsky's zone of proximal development, which keeps the teacher inside the prompt rather than the policy gradient. On hard questions, ZPPO constructs two reformulated prompts: a Binary Candidate-included Question (BCQ) pairs one correct teacher response with one incorrect student response as anonymized candidates the student must discriminate, and a Negative Candidate-included Question (NCQ) aggregates the student's wrong rollouts into a single prompt to surface their shared failure modes. A prompt replay buffer recirculates each hard question until it either graduates-the student's mean rollout accuracy on it reaches half- or is FIFO-evicted under finite capacity, amplifying BCQ and NCQ inside the student's current zone of proximal development. On the Qwen3.5 family at four student scales (0.8B-9B) with a 27B teacher, post-trained as vision-language models and evaluated on a 31-benchmark suite (16 VLM, 10 LLM, 5 Video), ZPPO outperforms off/on-policy distillation and GRPO, with the largest gains at the smallest scale.

</details>


### [50] [Darshana Graph: A Parallel Commentary Corpus for Comparative Indian Philosophy, with Stylometric and Exploratory Graph Analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18222)
*Joy Bose*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Darshana Graph，这是一个包含超过12.5万条印度哲学文本的数字化语料库，核心亮点是对8500条经文进行了跨18位评论家的对齐处理，并验证了通过风格计量分析和LLM知识图谱提取来研究复杂哲学流派的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 印度哲学史上的经典文本通常伴随着多个学派的深度评论，但目前缺乏大规模、结构化的多学派评论对比数据集。作者旨在构建一个包含跨传统、跨评论对齐的语料库，以解决学界在定量研究不同哲学解释传统如何解读同一核心经文方面的资源匮乏问题。

Method: 本文采用了以下方法：1. 语料库构建：从经典印度教、佛教和耆那教文本中汇编超过12.5万条记录，并对其中8500条核心经文进行18位历史评论家的跨版本对齐；2. 风格计量分析：不依赖机器学习，通过引用密度、反驳率和句子复杂度等指标量化论证风格；3. LLM知识提取：构建了一个包含预定义关系词表和确定性事后验证机制的大语言模型管道，旨在从文本中提取结构化的哲学概念关系。

Result: 研究结果显示：1. 风格计量分析发现引用密度与反驳率之间存在适度的负相关，并揭示了特定宗派内部反驳率的显著提升；2. 知识提取实验表明，LLM管道能够构建跨学派的争议模式图谱，但也暴露了当前模型在处理复杂哲学逻辑时存在的提取局限性（如与嵌入分析结果的不一致）。

Conclusion: Darshana Graph 为跨学派、跨评论的印度哲学研究提供了重要的数字基础设施。通过整合与结构化历史文献，该资源不仅支持对复杂哲学论证风格的定量分析，还展示了利用大语言模型从哲学文本中提取知识图谱的潜力与局限。该数据集为数字人文研究提供了弥足珍贵的跨文化、跨传统分析语料。

Abstract: We introduce Darshana Graph, a corpus of over 125,000 text records spanning classical Hindu, Buddhist, and Jain philosophical traditions, drawn from public-domain and openly licensed translations of sources including the Bhagavad Gita, Brahma Sutras, principal Upanishads, the Pali Canon, and core Jain texts. Its distinctive contribution lies in a structurally unique subset of roughly 8,500 Hindu and Jain records in which the same root verse or sutra is aligned across eighteen historical commentators representing five schools of Vedanta and other darshanas, enabling direct comparison of how independent interpretive traditions read identical source material. To our knowledge, no publicly available resource provides comparable cross-commentator alignment at this scale. We present two analyses built on this corpus. First, a transparent stylometric comparison requiring no machine learning measures argumentative style through scriptural citation density, explicit refutation rate, and sentence complexity. It finds a moderate negative correlation between citation density and refutation rate, a marked increase in refutation rate across three commentators in a related doctrinal lineage, and measurable genre-level differences within the Pali Canon itself. Second, we describe a constrained large language model pipeline that extracts typed philosophical relationships between concepts using a predefined relation vocabulary and deterministic post-hoc validation. The resulting graph surfaces cross-school disagreement patterns while also revealing important extraction limitations, including cases where an independent embedding-based analysis disagrees with the graph-derived findings. We release the full corpus, extracted relationship graph, and all source code.

### [51] [ReproRepo: Scaling Reproducibility Audits with GitHub Repository Issues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18237)
*Shanda Li,Qiuhong Anna Wei,Jingwu Tang,Valerie Chen,Nihar B Shah,Tim Dettmers,Yiming Yang,Ameet Talwalkar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 作者推出了 ReproRepo 框架，通过利用 GitHub 上的真实复现问题，自动化评估大模型代理在学术科研复现中的辅助能力，并证实了该方法在处理大规模论文集时的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的科研复现评估基准依赖大量的人工整理与评估，难以规模化。为了解决这一痛点，作者希望利用自然存在的 GitHub 问题数据，构建一个可扩展的、自动化的框架来评估大模型在辅助科研复现中的实际表现。

Method: 提出 ReproRepo 框架，利用真实世界的 GitHub 问题（即人类开发者报告的复现障碍）作为自然监督信号；在 1,149 篇机器学习论文上对四种前沿大模型代理配置进行了评估，通过语义相关性分析评估代理识别复现问题的准确性。

Result: 实验发现，表现最好的大模型代理（Codex + GPT-5.5）能为约 90% 的研究论文识别出至少一个语义相关的真实复现障碍；代理在识别可见故障和定位语义范围方面表现出色，但在具体代码路径的精确归因定位上仍有提升空间。

Conclusion: ReproRepo 是一个可扩展的自动化评估框架，通过利用真实的 GitHub 问题来评估大模型代理在复现研究中的能力。研究表明，尽管大模型在精确定位方面仍有不足，但它们在识别真实世界复现障碍方面表现出极高的潜力，可作为未来学术复现审计的重要工具。

Abstract: Reproducing research results from papers and released code is central to scientific progress. Existing works have introduced benchmarks to evaluate whether LLM agents can assist with reproducibility, but they are difficult to scale due to their reliance on substantial manual effort for data curation and evaluation. We introduce ReproRepo, a scalable framework for reproducibility evaluation that leverages human-raised GitHub issues as naturally occurring supervision on realistic reproduction blockers. We instantiate ReproRepo on 1,149 recent machine learning papers from major conferences and evaluate four frontier model-agent configurations. Our results show that LLM agents, even without executing code, can identify many real-world reproducibility problems from paper-repository pairs: the best agent in our study, namely Codex with GPT-5.5, surfaces at least one semantically related human-reported blocker for ~90% of papers in the study. Further analysis shows that agents are particularly effective for surfacing visible failures and identifying the right semantic region, but may still be insufficient in exact localization. ReproRepo can serve as a reusable, scalable framework for future evaluations of LLM agents on real-world reproducibility auditing. Our code is released at https://github.com/LithiumDA/ReproRepo.

</details>


### [52] [Variable-Width Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18246)
*Zhaofeng Wu,Oliver Sieberling,Shawn Tan,Rameswar Panda,Yury Polyanskiy,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非均匀宽度分配的“> <former”架构，通过在网络中间层进行缩窄，在保持同等模型规模的同时，显著提升了语言模型性能，并降低了计算量和内存开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Transformer架构大多采用恒定宽度，这意味着所有层被分配了相同的计算和参数资源。然而，不同深度的层在模型中可能承担着不同的功能。研究者旨在探索通过改变网络深度的宽度分配（即非均匀分配）来更有效地利用参数和计算预算，以提高模型性能并降低计算开销。

Method: 提出了一种名为“> <former”的架构，通过非均匀的宽度分配策略改变了Transformer的层结构：保持网络首尾两层较宽，而将中间层设为较窄，形成“X”形布局。同时，引入了一种无需额外参数的残差调整机制（residual resizing mechanism）来处理不同宽度层之间的连接。

Result: 实验表明，“> <former”在200M到3B参数规模的语言模型上，均优于参数量相同的均匀宽度基准模型。该架构减少了约22%的FLOPs消耗，并降低了约15%的KV Cache显存占用和I/O成本。分析显示，这种瓶颈结构促使残差流产生了质量上不同的表征。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了非均匀的宽度分配（即“X”形架构）是一种更高效的模型缩放策略。通过减少计算冗余并优化资源分配，该架构在参数量相同的情况下实现了更好的性能，同时降低了计算成本和推理时的显存占用，为未来设计更高效的大语言模型提供了新的思路。

Abstract: Scaling model size, specifically depth and width, has driven significant progress in transformer-based language models. However, most architectures maintain a constant width across all layers, allocating a fixed parameter and computation budget evenly despite different layers potentially playing distinct computational roles. In this work, we empirically investigate nonuniform capacity allocation across network depth by proposing a $\times$-shaped > <former architecture. This design maintains wider early and late layers while narrowing the middle layers, utilizing a parameter-free residual resizing mechanism. Across decoder-only language models ranging from 200M to 2B parameters (dense) and 3B parameters (MoE), our > <former consistently outperforms parameter-matched uniform baselines on language modeling loss. By reducing the average layer width, this architecture also requires fewer overall FLOPs (22% reduction under fitted loss-matched scaling curves) and smaller KV cache memory and I/O cost (15% reduction). In analysis, we show that this bottleneck structure results in qualitatively different representations in residual streams. Overall, our results demonstrate that nonuniform width allocation can result in more resource-optimal scaling of language models.

</details>


<div id='cs.IR'></div>

# cs.IR [[Back]](#toc)

### [53] [On the Memorization Behavior of LLMs in Generative Recommendation: Observations, Implications, and Training Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17276)
*Sunwoo Kim,Sunkyung Lee,Clark Mingxuan Ju,Donald Loveland,Bhuvesh Kumar,Kijung Shin,Neil Shah,Liam Collins*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文揭示了生成式推荐中LLM过度依赖“一跳”记忆的问题，并提出了IIRG训练策略，通过显式学习多跳协同与语义关系，有效提升了模型在复杂推荐场景下的泛化性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型（LLM）的生成式推荐系统虽然表现出色，但往往过度依赖训练数据中的“一跳”记忆（即直接推荐训练集中已有的后续项）。这种过度记忆现象限制了LLM利用预训练知识进行更广泛的推理，使得模型在面对训练集中未包含的长尾或复杂推荐场景时性能欠佳。

Method: 本文提出了IIRG（Item-Item Relation-aware Generation）训练策略。该方法通过两类知识增强模型：(1) 基于多跳协同关系的项-项关系，捕捉用户行为序列中的全局协作信号；(2) 基于项目主题相似性的语义关系，弥补仅依赖行为序列带来的稀疏性问题。通过将这些关系整合进训练过程，引导模型超越简单的记忆模式。

Result: 实验表明，LLM在生成式推荐中的大部分性能增益实际上源于对“一跳”记忆的利用。IIRG策略显著优于仅使用标准下一项预测训练的基准模型，特别是在那些无法通过训练集中一跳路径预测的目标用户群体中，性能提升尤为显著。

Conclusion: 本文指出单纯的下一项预测任务会导致LLM在推荐系统中过度依赖“一跳”记忆（one-hop memorization）。通过IIRG策略显式地注入跨多跳的协同关系和语义关系，能够显著提升模型在非显式序列模式下的泛化能力，从而突破LLM在生成式推荐中的性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Generative recommendation (GR) has emerged as a promising direction for recommender systems. Recently, large language models (LLMs) have been increasingly adopted for GR, as their rich pretrained knowledge is expected to help them generalize beyond common user behavior patterns that traditional memorization-oriented baselines can capture. However, existing LLM-based GR works largely ignore LLMs' well-known tendency to memorize, which, if present in LLMs fine-tuned for GR, would restrict their utilization of pretrained knowledge. In this work, we investigate this concern by examining one-hop memorization, where a model recommends items that are direct successors of items in the training data. We show that LLMs do this more than non-LLM-based GR models-in fact, the vast majority of their gains over GR baselines are actually on users whose target items can be predicted through one-hop memorization. We intuit that improving performance on the remaining users requires LLMs to learn richer item-item relations beyond one-hop transitions. To achieve this, we propose IIRG, a novel training strategy that teaches LLMs to capture: (1) collaborative relations derived from item co-occurrences across multiple hops in user sequences, and (2) semantic relations among items with similar themes, both of which can serve as useful recommendation signals. We show that IIRG significantly improves over LLMs trained solely with standard next-item prediction, with especially large gains for users whose test items are not covered by train-time one-hop transitions.

</details>


### [54] [RSRank: Learning Relevance from Representational Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17468)
*Archit Gupta,Sai Sundaresan,Debabrata Mahapatra*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对现有RAG重排序器依赖启发式阈值及Logit信号评估不准的问题，本文提出了一种基于“表示偏移（RS）”的轻量级重排序框架，通过对齐查询的内在状态变化来精准评估文档相关性，实现了更好的性能与更简便的部署。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于RAG的系统中，重排序环节往往依赖经验阈值，且现有的基于语言模型Logit信号的打分方式并非专门针对相关性评估设计，导致过滤效果和准确性受限。因此，研究旨在寻找一种更具原则性和鲁棒性的相关性评估信号，以替代传统的启发式方法。

Method: 研究者提出利用查询在给定文档条件下的“表示偏移（RS）”作为相关性度量指标。他们观察到候选文档诱导的RS与理想文档集诱导的RS之间的对齐程度是判断相关性的稳健信号，并据此设计了一个轻量级训练框架，通过学习映射将RS转化为校准后的相关性分数，从而实现零阈值的无效内容过滤。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在多个检索数据集上均优于现有的前沿重排序模型，且得益于其固有的过滤特性，显著降低了对启发式阈值调优的依赖，验证了表示偏移在相关性排序中的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过引入表示偏移（RS）作为相关性信号，该研究提供了一种更具解释性和鲁棒性的排序方法。其训练框架能够生成校准后的相关性分数，有效简化了阈值调优的复杂性，并提升了检索系统的整体性能。

Abstract: As enterprises deploy RAG-based systems to provide grounded responses to user queries, reranking has become a critical component for the final filtering step that separates relevant from distracting or irrelevant documents. Existing rerankers often rely on heuristic thresholds to achieve optimal filtering. Moreover, for relevance scoring, state-of-the-art methods use a language model's logit signals, which are designed for next-token prediction, not for assessing relevance. To address these limitations, we identify a principled signal for relevance: the representational shift (RS) induced in a query's internal state when conditioned on a document. We observe that the alignment between (a) RS induced by a candidate document and (b) RS induced by an oracle document-set provides a robust indicator of relevance. Building on this insight, we introduce a lightweight training framework that learns projections mapping RS to calibrated relevance scores. Our training objectives naturally filter irrelevant content at a zero threshold, reducing dependence on heuristic tuning. Across diverse retrieval datasets, our method delivers gains over SOTA rerankers.

</details>


### [55] [Temporal Preference Optimization for Unsupervised Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17664)
*HyunJin Kim,Jaejun Shim,Young Jin Kim,JinYeong Bak*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为TPOUR的无监督时间检索增强框架，通过引入TRPO偏好优化方法和时间嵌入插值技术，在无需显式标注的情况下，显著提升了检索器在跨时间周期任务中的时间对齐能力与检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无监督密集检索器虽然具备可扩展性，但在处理跨时间跨度的文档集时，难以捕捉查询与文档之间的时间相关性，导致检索结果出现时间偏差（例如将不同年份的同名事件混淆）。此外，现有解决该问题的方法往往依赖于昂贵的显式时间戳标注数据。

Method: 1. 提出了时间检索偏好优化（TRPO）训练方法，将偏好学习应用于时间维度，引导检索器偏向时间对齐的文档；
2. 引入了基于时间嵌入插值的机制，使模型能够泛化到未见的时间段，实现连续的时间对齐。

Result: 在时间信息检索（T-IR）任务中，TPOUR表现优于现有的无监督和有监督基线。在显著更小（约72.7倍）的情况下，TPOUR Contriever相较于Qwen-Embedding-8B，在显式和隐式查询中的平均nDCG@5指标分别提升了4.04（+12.15%）和4.98（+15.21%）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的TPOUR框架成功解决了无监督密集检索器在处理时间相关性时的局限性。通过引入TRPO方法，该框架能够在无需显式标注时间戳的情况下，有效利用时间维度上的偏好学习，在保持模型轻量化的同时，显著提升了时间信息检索任务的性能，并具备良好的时间泛化能力。

Abstract: Unsupervised dense retrievers offer scalability by learning semantic similarity from unlabeled documents via contrastive learning, but they struggle to capture the temporal relevance, retrieving semantically related but temporally misaligned documents-an important aspect when a document collection spans multiple time periods (e.g., retrieving documents from 2018-2025 for "Who is the president in 2019?" introduces temporal ambiguity). Existing methods rely on supervised training with explicit timestamps, which are not always feasible. We propose TPOUR (Temporal Preference Optimization for Unsupervised Retriever), which uses our novel training method Temporal Retrieval Preference Optimization (TRPO). TRPO reinterprets preference learning in the temporal dimension, guiding the retriever to favor temporally aligned documents. TPOUR further generalizes to unseen time periods via interpolation in a learned time embedding, enabling continuous temporal alignment. Experiments on temporal information retrieval (T-IR), TPOUR outperforms both unsupervised and supervised baselines. Compared to Qwen-Embedding-8B, despite being about 72.7x smaller, TPOUR Contriever improves average nDCG@5 by +4.04 (+12.15%) on explicit and +4.98 (+15.21%) on implicit queries. We provide our code at https://github.com/agwaBom/TPOUR.

</details>


### [56] [Do Generative Recommenders Deepen the Information Cocoon? A Closed-Loop Simulation with LLM-powered User Simulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17707)
*Jiyuan Yang,Gengxin Sun,Mengqi Zhang,Lingjie Wang,Yuanzi Li,Hongxi Cui,Xin Xin,Pengjie Ren*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文通过 RecLoop 框架对比了生成式与传统推荐系统，发现生成式推荐系统在减轻信息茧房方面表现更优，但其效果深受 Tokenization 方法和模型规模的影响，并非完全免疫。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究生成式推荐系统（基于语义 ID，即 SID）在反馈循环中是否会加剧信息茧房现象，并分析其与传统序列推荐在信息茧房形成机制上的异同。

Method: 提出名为 RecLoop 的闭环模拟框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）驱动的用户代理进行多次反馈循环模拟；除了传统的曝光度指标，还引入了“代码空间结构茧房”（Code-Space Structural Cocoon）这一模型层级指标来衡量生成的 SID 空间集中度。

Result: 实验表明生成式推荐比传统基线更不容易产生曝光层面的信息茧房；但在生成的 SID 空间内仍会发生集中现象。茧房严重程度与 Tokenization 策略（协作信号比语义标记化更易产生茧房）和模型规模（模型越大多样性越好）高度相关。

Conclusion: 生成式推荐系统在缓解信息茧房方面优于传统序列推荐，但其茧房效应仍受物品标记化策略（Tokenization）和模型规模的影响。协作信号标记化会加剧茧房效应，而更大的模型有助于保持代码空间多样性并保留对小众内容的访问。

Abstract: Recommender systems alleviate information overload, yet repeated feedback between recommendations and user interactions can reinforce existing preferences and narrow users' exposure, forming information cocoons. While this phenomenon has been widely studied in traditional sequential recommendation, its impact on generative recommendation remains unclear. By replacing atomic item IDs with Semantic ID (SID) sequences, generative recommenders introduce a different recommendation mechanism whose role in information cocoon formation is not yet understood. To investigate whether generative recommenders deepen information cocoons, we propose \textsc{RecLoop}, a closed-loop simulation framework with LLM-driven user agents. We compare two generative recommenders and two traditional sequential baselines on two Amazon datasets across multiple feedback cycles. In addition to standard exposure-level metrics, we introduce \emph{Code-Space Structural Cocoon}, a model-level metric that measures concentration in the generated SID space. Experimental results show that generative recommenders are generally less prone to exposure-level cocoon formation than traditional baselines, preserving broader exposure diversity and slowing cross-user homogenization. However, feedback loops can still induce concentration within the generated SID space. We further find that cocoon severity depends strongly on tokenization strategy and model scale: collaborative-signal tokenization produces stronger cocoon effects than semantic tokenization, whereas larger models maintain greater code-space diversity and better retain access to niche content. These findings suggest that information cocoons in generative recommendation are shaped not only by recommendation behavior, but also by item tokenization and model capacity. Our code is available at https://github.com/Dregen-Yor/RecLoop.

</details>


### [57] [Understanding and Debugging Failures in N-Gram-Based Generative Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17721)
*Richard Takacs,Adrian Bracher,Svitlana Vakulenko*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文探讨了生成式检索（GR）的故障模式，构建了故障分类体系，分析了ngram类方法（如SEAL、MINDER）的常见错误，并开发了一款辅助分析GR模型行为的Web工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式检索（GR）虽然利用语言模型展示了独特优势，但也引入了新的故障机制。目前学术界对GR系统的错误行为缺乏系统性理解，亟需对其故障模式进行深入研究和分析。

Method: 1. 文献综述：基于现有文献，构建了生成式检索故障模式的分类法（Taxonomy）。2. 实验分析：针对ngram类GR方法（SEAL和MINDER）进行实证研究，分析其在检索过程中的错误表现。3. 工具开发：设计并发布了一款Web可视化分析工具，用于追踪生成的ngram及其对最终排序结果的影响。

Result: 研究发现GR系统存在以下关键问题：1. 文档标识符（docid）存在歧义性；2. 标识符生成的多样性较低；3. 特定标识符对检索结果具有不成比例的影响力。此外，作者提供的新工具能够有效帮助开发者直观识别GR模型在检索过程中的失误点。

Conclusion: 本文通过对生成式检索（GR）中以ngram为基础的方法（如SEAL和MINDER）进行深入分析，揭示了其独特的故障模式。研究强调了建立系统性分类法和开发可视化工具对于理解GR系统行为及提升未来检索模型鲁棒性的重要性。

Abstract: Generative Retrieval (GR) is an emerging Information Retrieval (IR) paradigm that is motivated by increasingly capable language models. In GR, a model directly generates identifiers for relevant documents. While these systems offer unique advantages, they also introduce distinct failure mechanisms. We explore these failure modes in three contributions: (1) We present a taxonomy of GR failure modes based on GR literature. (2) We empirically investigate failure in a subset of GR: ngram-based methods, more specifically, SEAL and MINDER. Our analysis reveals common issues, such as ambiguous docids, low identifier diversity, and the disproportionate impact of specific identifiers. (3) We introduce a new web-based tool that helps the IR community analyze generated ngrams and their respective contribution to the final ranking, providing an intuitive interface to identify where such GR methods go wrong.

### [58] [Non-negative Elastic Net Decoding for Information Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17910)
*Koki Okajima,Yasutoshi Ida,Tsukasa Yoshida,Yasuaki Nakamura*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对传统密集检索容易出现结果冗余的问题，本文提出了一种非负弹性网络（NNN）解码方法，通过将检索建模为联合解码问题，有效提升了检索结果的多样性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的密集检索（Dense Retrieval）仅依赖查询与单个文档嵌入的点积来计算得分，忽略了语料库整体内容的上下文信息，导致检索结果中常出现语义高度相似且冗余的内容，缺乏多样性。

Method: 本文提出了一种非负弹性网络（NNN）解码方法，将检索视作一个联合解码问题。该方法旨在选择一组能够通过稀疏非负线性组合重构查询嵌入的文档，以此在考虑语料库上下文的前提下实现多样化检索；此外，作者还引入了针对NNN解码优化的端到端训练流程。

Result: 理论上，证明了NNN解码能够完全覆盖传统密集检索的正确查询，并在存在冗余文档的语料库中表现更优；实验表明，在冻结的嵌入上使用NNN解码能提升检索性能，且通过端到端训练优化后的嵌入在所有指标和基准测试上均显著超越了传统的密集检索。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入NNN解码范式，突破了传统密集检索中仅依赖点积计算导致检索结果冗余的局限性，证明了联合解码在提升检索多样性和准确性方面的巨大潜力，为信息检索领域提供了一种更优的特征利用策略。

Abstract: Dense retrieval has become the dominant paradigm in information retrieval, in which each document is scored against a query by the inner product of their vector embeddings, and the top-$k$ documents by score are retrieved for this query. However, since each document's score depends solely on the embedding of the query and itself, the retrieval process is oblivious to the content of the entire corpus. Therefore, dense retrieval cannot avoid selecting semantically similar documents from the corpus, which may result in a non-diverse, redundant set of retrieved documents. To this end, we approach retrieval as a joint decoding problem, in which documents are selected as a set with regard to the context of the rest of the corpus. To achieve this, we propose Non-Negative elastic Net (NNN) decoding, which selects documents whose embeddings jointly reconstruct the query embedding as a sparse non-negative linear combination.
  Our main theoretical result establishes a strict separation between dense retrieval and NNN decoding. For any corpus, every query correctly handled by dense retrieval is also handled by NNN decoding, while on corpora containing correlated documents, NNN decoding additionally handles queries that dense retrieval cannot. Experimental results indicate that applying NNN decoding to frozen embeddings trained for inner-product scoring yields consistent improvements across several benchmarks. Moreover, we introduce an end-to-end training procedure which optimizes the embeddings for NNN decoding, producing significant performance gains surpassing in all metrics and benchmarks compared to dense retrieval. Our work establishes a new paradigm for leveraging dense embeddings in information retrieval, beyond the standard practice of inner-product scoring.

</details>


### [59] [IUU+DB: Tracking Illegal, Unreported, and Unregulated Fishing, Seafood Fraud, and Labor Abuse through LLM-driven Information Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18181)
*Henry Bodwell,Hong Yang,John C. Simeone,Kelvin Gorospe,Bella Sullivan,Lana Huang,Jessica Gephart,Sandy Aylesworth,Molly Masterton,Naren Ramakrishnan*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于大语言模型的IUU+DB系统，旨在通过自动化提取和整合全球范围内的非法捕捞及相关犯罪事件数据，解决非法捕捞活动缺乏定量分析的难题，为相关研究和监管提供数据支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非法、未报告和无管制（IUU）捕捞定义较为狭窄，难以涵盖更广泛的环境和供应链贸易犯罪。此外，目前缺乏系统化的定量分析工具来梳理非法捕捞的频率、地理分布、物种和参与者等信息，导致相关治理和研究面临困难。

Method: 提出了一种基于大型语言模型（LLM）的自动化系统IUU+DB，用于处理异构文档。该系统能够识别非法捕捞相关事件，从文本中提取关键实体（如参与者、地点、物种、船只、违规行为及执法结果），并具备数据去重和趋势分析功能。

Result: 案例研究和验证结果表明，IUU+DB能够成功提取并组织复杂的非法捕捞信息，识别出非法捕捞的地理和行为热点，从而为政策制定、学术研究及供应链合规性评估提供实证支持。

Conclusion: IUU+DB系统通过自动化手段有效地整合了碎片化的非法捕捞数据，为学术研究、行业风险评估及政府执法提供了强有力的工具，有助于填补全球非法渔业活动定量分析的空白。

Abstract: Illegal, unreported, and unregulated fishing (IUU) traditionally refers to fishing activities that violate applicable laws or occur in areas that lack applicable laws. We propose the term IUU+ to capture a broader suite of fisheries sector environmental and associated supply chain trade-related crimes and behaviors. Although IUU+ activity is widely recognized as a serious threat to marine ecosystems, markets, and livelihoods, a quantitative understanding of these incidents, e.g., their frequency, geography, species, actors, and patterns in the type of illicit activity, remains difficult to obtain. We propose IUU+DB, a large language model driven system for building a global incident database of IUU+ activity. The system ingests heterogeneous documents, classifies whether they describe relevant incidents, extracts key data elements such as actors, locations, species, vessels, violations, and enforcement outcomes, and supports deduplication and trend analysis. Case studies and validation results show that IUU+DB can help organize fragmented evidence, surface geographic and behavioral hotspots, support fisheries-domain specific research in academia and non-government organizations, assist source and species risk assessments for industry, and provide support for policy implementation and targeted enforcement efforts to government agencies.

### [60] [Correct When Paired, Wrong When Split: Decoupling and Editing Modality-Specific Neurons in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17057)
*Tingchao Fu,Wenkai Wang,Fanxiao Li,Huadong Zhang,Jinhong Zhang,Dayang Li,Yunyun Dong,Renyang Liu,Wei Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型知识编辑中“跨模态更新不一致”的问题，本文提出了DECODE框架，通过对模态特定神经元进行解耦定位与定向更新，有效解决了该领域面临的解耦失效挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型知识编辑方法存在“编辑解耦失效”问题，即更新多模态输入下的知识后，模型在单模态输入下仍会输出过时的事实。这源于模型中实体知识并非统一存储，而是分散在不同的模态特定路径中。

Method: 提出了一种名为DECODE的新方法。该方法通过显式地解耦并定位与特定模态相关的神经元群组，针对性地对这些神经元进行知识更新，从而确保更新能够有效传播到各个模态回路中。

Result: 广泛的实验证明，DECODE方法在不同模态触发条件下均能实现有效的知识更新，显著缓解了编辑解耦失效现象，在多模态和单模态输入下均能保持编辑后知识的一致性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过明确解耦和定位特定模态的神经元群组，可以有效解决多模态大模型在知识编辑中的“解耦失效”问题，实现跨模态的一致性知识更新。

Abstract: Although Knowledge Editing provides an efficient mechanism for updating the knowledge of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), we find that current paradigms still suffer from an important yet remain underexplored issue : editing decoupling failure, where entity-related knowledge can be updated when the model is triggered by multimodal inputs (text--image query pairs), however, it often reverts to outdated pre-edit facts when the paired inputs are split into unimodal ones. Our in-depth empirical analysis reveals that the entity knowledge in MLLMs is not stored as a unified representation, but is instead distributed across disentangled modality-specific pathways. As a result, updates biased toward multimodal queries fail to propagate effectively to unimodal circuits. To bridge this gap, we propose DECODE, which explicitly disentangles and localizes modality-specific neuron groups for targeted knowledge. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DECODE consistently achieves effective knowledge updates under different modality triggers, thereby mitigating editing decoupling failures.

</details>


### [61] [Diagnosing and Repairing Shape-Prior Shortcuts in Long-Range Single-Shot Fringe Projection Profilometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17093)
*Adam Haroon,Anush Lakshman,Cody Fleming,Beiwen Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过机械解释性方法发现远距离单帧条纹投影测量网络主要依赖物体形状先验而非物理相位解码，并据此设计了PhiCalNet，通过架构层面的相位-深度映射修复了该缺陷，显著提升了测量精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于学习的单帧条纹投影轮廓测量法（FPP）多局限于近距离，在远距离应用中存在光强衰减导致的信噪比下降问题，且现有的深度神经网络架构往往未能真正解码条纹相位，而是倾向于利用物体形状先验来处理深度回归，导致模型泛化能力差。

Method: 1. 使用机械解释性方法（线性探测、Grad-CAM、离群分布测试）分析现有架构；2. 提出PhiCalNet架构：放弃直接预测深度，改为输出包裹相位，并通过一个固定的可微分校准层进行深度映射；3. 引入保形不确定性量化（UQ）对预测结果进行过滤；4. 在包含15,600张图像的远距离（1.5-2.1米）合成数据集上进行验证。

Result: PhiCalNet将物体平均绝对误差（MAE）从基准网络的14.54毫米降低至4.46毫米（提升约3.3倍）；通过像素级保形UQ剔除不确定性最高的5%像素后，模型RMSE进一步大幅提升，且诊断结果与MI分析高度一致。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了通过结合机械解释性（MI）和保形不确定性量化（UQ）进行诊断，可以发现单帧条纹投影轮廓测量法（FPP）在远距离应用中的架构缺陷。通过PhiCalNet架构，将物理模型（相位到深度）强制植入网络结构而非仅作为损失函数，能够从根本上解决深度学习模型依赖物体形状先验而非条纹相位解码的错误决策模式。

Abstract: Learning-based single-shot fringe projection profilometry (FPP) has been studied mostly at close range. The long-range regime (standoff beyond 1 m) remains largely unaddressed: inverse-square intensity falloff lowers fringe signal-to-noise ratio and degrades physical ground truth, the single-shot problem is ill-posed because fringe-order information is absent from one image, and these architectures have not been studied mechanistically. We present a diagnose-repair-verify study using mechanistic interpretability (MI) and conformal uncertainty quantification (UQ) as convergent diagnostics: they agree on one physical failure locus, driving and verifying an architectural repair. On a photorealistic synthetic benchmark (15,600 fringe images, 50 objects at 1.5-2.1 m), a best UNet baseline reaches 14.54 mm object mean absolute error (MAE). Three probes (linear probing, Grad-CAM, flat-plane out-of-distribution test) converge: the baseline solves the task via object-boundary shape priors rather than fringe-phase decoding. We repair this with PhiCalNet, which outputs wrapped phase rather than depth and applies a fixed differentiable calibration layer mapping phase to depth, removing the shape-prior solution from the hypothesis space architecturally rather than by a loss penalty. A physics-informed loss that enforces the same physics as a soft penalty on a depth-regressing network yields no measurable gain, isolating the architecture as the operative factor. PhiCalNet reduces object MAE 3.3x to 4.46 mm; the residual is carried by 0.103% of pixels at the +/-pi wrap discontinuity. Pixel-wise conformal UQ confirms the diagnosis: rejecting the top 5% of object pixels by snapshot disagreement cuts PhiCalNet RMSE by 64% (20.6->7.4 mm) versus 3.5% for the baseline. MI and UQ converge on the same failure locus.

</details>


### [62] [Informative Missingness to Generate Irregular Clinical Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17106)
*Hadi Mehdizavareh,Gabriele Santangelo,Giovanna Nicora,Simon Lebech Cichosz,Arianna Dagliati,Arijit Khan,Riccardo Bellazzi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在电子健康记录（EHR）中，实验室检查的非规律性缺失往往包含临床决策和患者生理状况的潜在信息（即非随机缺失，MNAR）。现有的研究常将缺失值视为预处理噪声，而本文旨在通过扩散模型直接对这些缺失模式进行建模，从而生成符合临床逻辑、能够反映医患互动规律的合成时间序列数据。

Method: 基于扩散模型（Diffusion Model）的生成框架。研究扩展了TimeDiff框架，通过互补的扩散目标函数，同时对连续的实验室检验值（Lab values）和离散的观测模式（即数据缺失情况，Missingness patterns）进行联合建模。通过对MIMIC-III数据进行4小时区间对齐和7天窗口分割处理，保留了临床时间序列的统计特征。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，扩散模型能够捕捉临床数据中生理特征与医生检测行为之间复杂的依赖关系（MNAR机制），为生成高质量合成医疗数据提供了新路径。该方法合成的数据集可作为训练临床基础模型的预训练先验，推动医疗领域“先验数据拟合网络”的发展。

Abstract: Laboratory tests in electronic health records are collected irregularly, and the absence of a test order can be as informative as the measurement itself. Such missingness reflects clinicians' decisions and patient physiology, making it important to model it directly rather than treat it as a preprocessing artifact. Here we present a diffusion-based approach for generating clinical time series that jointly models laboratory values and their observation patterns using the public Data Analytics Challenge on Missing Data Imputation (DACMI) benchmark derived from MIMIC-III. To preserve realistic sampling, we align chart times into 4-hour intervals and segment admissions into 7-day windows, producing trajectories that pair each lab value with a corresponding observation indicator. Standard transformations and normalization are applied to stabilize training. Our method extends the TimeDiff framework to learn continuous lab values and discrete missingness patterns through complementary diffusion objectives. Experiments show that the generated data closely match real patient trajectories across individual lab distributions and joint value-missingness embeddings, demonstrating that diffusion models can capture clinically meaningful dependencies between patient physiology and clinicians' testing behavior under MNAR-like (missing-not-at-random) missingness. These preliminary results indicate that our model can serve as an initial component toward developing clinical foundation models. By producing synthetic priors that preserve key physiology-missingness relationships, this work motivates the subsequent training of Prior-Data Fitted Networks capable of leveraging informative missingness, which we will investigate in the extended work.

### [63] [Models Take Notes at Prefill: KV Cache Can Be Editable and Composable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17107)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大模型推理主要依赖缓存的“结论笔记”而非实时处理 KV 向量的机制。通过直接编辑与拼接缓存，无需完整重计算即可实现高效的动态上下文更新与技能迁移，显著提升了推理速度并兼容现有架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的前缀缓存（Prefix Caching）因其“全或无”的特性，一旦上下文发生微小变动就会导致整个缓存失效，从而造成巨大的重计算开销。本文旨在解决这一低效问题，探索如何通过重用大部分已有缓存来实现高效的动态上下文处理。

Method: 研究人员发现大模型在预填充阶段已将特定字段的条件结论写入下游 KV 缓存，而该字段自身的 KV 向量对决策影响极小。基于此，团队开发了两种新技术：1) 针对性编辑（Editable）：通过修正缓存中的关键点实现上下文更新；2) 组合化（Composable）：通过旋转位置编码（RoPE）重定位将“预编译技能”拼接至任意上下文。两者结合形成一种通用的编辑与组合代理。

Result: 实验证明，该方法在多个模型系列（包括 MoE 和多模态模型）上实现了与全量重计算几乎一致的输出（Logit 余弦相似度高达 0.90-0.999）。在在线 vLLM 基准测试中，该方法保持了 98.5% 的前缀缓存命中率，并将首字延迟（p90 TTFT）降低了 53 至 398 倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于缓存编辑与组合的新范式，证明了模型推理本质上是“已记忆结论的笔记”处理过程。通过该方法，不仅实现了高效的上下文更新与技能组合，还极大地降低了首字延迟（TTFT），且与现有的前缀缓存机制完全兼容。

Abstract: Prefix caching reuses prefill only across an exactly shared prefix, so one changed field invalidates the entire downstream cache. Yet overwriting the field's own key/value vectors and reusing the rest leaves the model acting on the old value. The reason, established causally across four model families: at prefill the model has already written the field-conditioned conclusion onto downstream notes; the field's own key/value drives under 1% of the decision. Read as a notebook of memoized conclusions, two capabilities follow. (1) It is editable. A salient erratum amends the notes; and with chain-of-thought, editing the field alone recovers the decision (1.00 at 8B, ~1% compute), while without CoT it is ignored. (2) It is composable. The notes are position-portable, so a precompiled skill can be RoPE-repositioned and spliced into any context, indistinguishable from full recompute (logit cosine 0.90-0.999, twelve models) at O(L) rather than O(L^2) time-to-first-token. A unified edit+compose agent stays decision-identical to recompute at up to 14.9x lower latency. The approach applies to any per-token attention KV cache, validated across scale, quantization, Mixture-of-Experts, and multimodal caches, and extends to several attention variants through small adapters. Because the erratum is append-only, it composes with production prefix caching: in an online vLLM benchmark it keeps the prefix cache-aligned (98.5% hit-rate), cutting p90 time-to-first-token by 53-398x.

</details>


### [64] [The Critical Role of Model Selection in Causal Inference: A Comparative Analysis of Classification Models within the InferBERT Framework for Pharmacovigilance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17113)
*Csaba Kiss,Roland Molontay,Gabriele Pergola*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究通过对比评估发现，在药物不良事件的因果检测中，针对医学领域预训练的模型（BioBERT）优于大型语言模型，证明了领域专业性比单纯的模型规模对药物警戒任务更为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 药物警戒中区分因果药物不良事件（ADEs）与伪相关是核心挑战。现有InferBERT框架虽结合了Transformer模型与Do-calculus，但模型选择的影响尚不明确。本研究旨在探讨模型复杂度、领域特定预训练、规模效应（LLM）及校准技术对因果关系检测效果的影响。

Method: 研究评估了四种不同类型的模型（XGBoost、ALBERT、BioBERT、Med-LLaMA）在InferBERT框架下的表现。通过在两个基准数据集（AILF和TRAM）上进行5折交叉验证（重复20次），对比了它们的准确率、预期校准误差（ECE）以及与传统药物警戒信号（PRR, ROR, EBGM）的Jaccard一致性，并分析了后验校准的影响。

Result: BioBERT在两个数据集上均取得了最高的准确率，并与传统药物警戒信号具有最强的一致性。Med-LLaMA尽管规模较大，但在任务中表现不佳。研究证实，领域特定的预训练对提升因果检测性能具有决定性作用，而模型校准虽能改善ECE，但对准确率和因果发现的影响并不一致。

Conclusion: 在药物警戒领域，模型性能的关键在于领域特定的预训练，而非单纯的模型规模。相较于大型语言模型（LLM），针对特定医学领域优化的中等规模模型（如BioBERT）在因果药物不良事件检测中表现更为优异，且能更好地与传统警戒指标保持一致。

Abstract: Distinguishing causal adverse drug events (ADEs) from spurious correlations remains a central challenge in pharmacovigilance. The InferBERT framework integrates transformer models with Do-calculus, but its success hinges on the underlying classification model. This study evaluates the impact of model choice in InferBERT, assessing whether simpler models suffice, if domain-specific pre-training helps, whether scaling to LLMs improves causal detection, and the effect of post-hoc calibration. We performed a comparative study on two benchmarks: Analgesics-induced Acute Liver Failure (AILF) and Tramadol-related Mortalities (TRAM). Four models were evaluated-XGBoost (baseline), ALBERT (original InferBERT), BioBERT (biomedical transformer), and Med-LLaMA (medical LLM)-using 5-fold cross-validation repeated over 20 runs. We measured accuracy, Expected Calibration Error (ECE) pre- and post-isotonic regression, and Jaccard concordance of causal terms with PRR, ROR, and EBGM; significance was tested with paired t-tests. BioBERT achieved the highest accuracy on both datasets, while Med-LLaMA underperformed despite its size and parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Domain-specific pre-training was decisive. Calibration improved ECE but had mixed effects on accuracy and causal discovery. BioBERT's superiority also yielded the strongest concordance with traditional pharmacovigilance signals. These results show that domain-specific pre-training provides a clear advantage over simpler baselines and larger LLMs. Investing in manageable, domain-aware models is more effective for computational pharmacovigilance than simply scaling model size.

Abstract: Foundation models (FMs) have emerged as powerful representation extractors for medical data, yet their generalizability to datasets under distribution shift remains underexplored. This work systematically evaluates FM-based representations on a suite of computational pathology tasks across two real-world commercial cohorts, IH-BC and IH-NSCLC, drawn from the licensed in-house (IH) oncology dataset. The trustworthiness of selected unimodal and multimodal pipelines is further assessed through conformal prediction. Our results show that FM representations achieve competitive performance on out-of-distribution data and that multimodal fusion helps mainly when no single modality dominates the signal. Conformal prediction reveals that in the majority of cases where a point prediction fails, the true diagnosis remains recoverable within the prediction set, reinforcing the value of uncertainty-aware inference for clinical support.

### [66] [MODE: Modality-Decomposed Expert-Level Mixed-Precision Quantization for MoE Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17118)
*Yuanteng Chen,Peisong Wang,Zhilei Liu,Nanxin Zeng,Yuantian Shao,Shiqiang Lang,Tao Liu,Chuangyi Li,Qinghao Hu,Gang Li,Jing Liu,Jian Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对MoE-MLLM量化中的专家重要性评估偏差问题，本文提出MODE框架，通过解耦模态选择频率及过滤冗余视觉信息，实现了更优的混合精度量化，显著降低了显存开销并保持了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE-MLLM虽然性能卓越，但显存开销巨大，现有针对MoE-LLM的专家级量化方法在应用到多模态模型时表现不佳。主要原因是现有方法忽视了跨模态和模态内部的偏差：视觉Token数量占据绝对优势导致专家选择频率偏差，且大量冗余视觉Token进一步干扰了对关键视觉特征专家的识别。

Method: 提出了一种名为MODE的模态解耦专家级混合精度量化框架：1. 实施跨模态专家选择频率解耦，消除视觉Token对文本重要专家选择的遮蔽；2. 过滤冗余视觉Token以获取去噪的视觉频率统计；3. 引入模态敏感度评估作为补充信号；4. 将上述多维信号整合进整数线性规划（ILP）模型，以在给定约束下优化专家的比特位宽分配。

Result: 在W3A16（3位权重量化，16位激活）设置下，该方法将平均性能损失控制在2.9%以内，并在极端2位量化设置下取得了显著的性能提升，表现优于现有的量化方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的MODE框架有效地解决了MoE-MLLM在量化过程中专家重要性评估偏差的问题，通过模态解耦和冗余视觉Token过滤，实现了更精确的比特位宽分配，为大规模多模态模型的轻量化部署提供了高效且鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts Multimodal Large Language Models (MoE-MLLMs) offer remarkable performance but incur prohibitive GPU memory costs, making compression essential. Among PTQ methods, expert-level mixed-precision quantization has proven effective for MoE-LLMs, yet suffers notable degradation on MoE-MLLMs due to two overlooked biases in expert importance estimation. (1) At the cross-modal level, the numerical dominance of vision tokens causes expert selection frequency to be dominated by vision tokens, masking experts that are critical to the text modality; (2) at the intra-vision level, the large proportion of redundant vision tokens further skew frequency statistics, obscuring experts critical for informative visual content. To bridge gaps, we propose MODE, a modality-decomposed expert-level mixed-precision quantization framework for MoE-MLLMs that decomposes expert selection frequency by modality, filters redundant vision tokens to obtain denoised visual frequency, and further evaluates quantization sensitivity per modality as a complementary signal to frequency-based estimation. These signals are integrated into an Integer Linear Programming formulation to assign per-expert bit-widths under a given budget. Extensive experiments show that MODE is particularly well-suited for MoE-MLLMs, limiting average performance loss to within 2.9% at W3A16, with larger gains at the extreme 2-bit setting.

</details>


### [67] [Noise-Driven Escape from Metastable Phases explains Grokking in Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17120)
*Ibrahim Talha Ersoy,Karoline Wiesner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从统计物理视角解释了神经网络的“顿悟”现象：模型由于L2正则化形成了多个亚稳态，导致训练被困，直到SGD噪声使其跨越能垒，从而实现了从过拟合到泛化的突变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在揭示深度学习中“顿悟”（Grokking）现象的本质原因，即模型在经历长期明显的过拟合后，为何会突然实现泛化。作者希望通过相变和亚稳态的视角，解释神经网络在训练过程中如何被困在低准确率状态，并探索导致这种现象的物理机制。

Method: 研究者以线性深度神经网络（DNN）为模型，结合统计物理学方法，利用L2正则化来人为构建亚稳态，通过测量逃逸时间验证其是否遵循阿伦尼乌斯（Arrhenius）缩放，并利用稀疏子采样技术复现了典型的“顿悟”曲线。此外，作者还探讨了该机制在通用非线性DNN中的适用性。

Result: 实验证明，DNN的特征学习与L2正则化强度呈现一阶相变关系，且亚稳态的数量等于可学习特征的数量（即数据协方差矩阵奇异值的数量）。研究成功复现了“顿悟”式的延迟收敛现象，并证实了模型从亚稳态逃逸的过程符合物理学中的阿伦尼乌斯缩放规律。

Conclusion: 本文通过证明“顿悟”（Grokking）现象与L2正则化引起的一阶相变中的滞后效应一致，揭示了神经网络在训练过程中陷入亚稳态并最终通过随机梯度下降（SGD）噪声跨越能垒的物理机制，为理解深度学习的泛化提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) exhibit first order phase transitions under variations of the L2 regularization strength, with each transition marking the onset of a new learnable feature. Below a critical regularization strength, all features are in principle learnable, but coexisting metastable states, separated by energy barriers, can trap the network and impede convergence. A strength of DNNs is their ability to generalize. But many open questions remain, among them the origin of so called grokking: the abrupt, delayed onset of generalization after prolonged apparent overfitting. We show for linear DNNs that grokking is consistent with hysteresis in first-order L2 phase transitions: using L2 regularization to engineer deliberate trapping, we demonstrate that a model in a low-accuracy metastable state escapes only when SGD noise drives it across an energy barrier, with escape times following Arrhenius scaling. We reproduce grokking-like delayed convergence across two orders of magnitude in escape time by deliberately trapping models in metastable phases. Using sparse sub-sampling we also reproduce the canonical grokking curve where test error eventually approaches the final training error. Our work suggests that the number of metastable states equals the number of learnable features -- one per singular value of the data covariance -- the potential for hysteresis grows naturally with task complexity. We provide evidence that the same mechanism likely operates in general nonlinear DNNs. Our results provide routes toward more efficient learning schemes.

</details>


### [68] [Towards Fast GNN Surrogates for CO2 Migration in Complex Geological Formations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17180)
*Rodrigo S. Luna,Thiago H. N. Coelho,Luiz S. L. Neto,Roberto M. Velho,Adriano M. A. Cortes,Renato N. Elias,Alexandre G. Evsukoff,Fernando A. Rochinha,Mauricio Araya-Polo,Herve Gross,Alvaro L. G. A. Coutinho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图神经网络的机器学习代理模型，专门用于高效预测地质储层中CO2羽流的运移，通过引入各向异性消息传递机制，该模型在保持计算效率的同时，能够准确捕捉复杂多相流的物理特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的数值模拟在预测复杂地质结构中多相流（如CO2羽流运移）时计算成本高昂。本研究旨在开发一种数据驱动的机器学习替代模型，以在保证计算效率的同时，准确复现多相流的关键物理行为，如尖锐的气液界面、强对流传输和指进现象。

Method: 提出了一种端到端图神经网络（GNN）代理模型：1. 将计算单元建模为图中的节点，通过基于传导率和几何属性的边来编码物理相互作用；2. 设计了各向异性消息传递机制，根据几何特征偏向物理相关的传输方向；3. 在潜在空间中使用自回归残差公式进行时间演化建模，并采用多步监督训练。

Result: 在SPE11A基准测试中，该模型成功预测了关键监测指标（气体饱和度和液相密度），即使在较长的预测周期内，累积误差也保持在适中水平，展示了其在复杂物理场景下的竞争力和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了端到端图神经网络代理模型在模拟复杂地质结构中CO2羽流运移方面的有效性。通过引入各向异性消息传递机制和自回归残差建模，该方法能够捕捉多相流中的关键物理特征，为地质储层监测提供了一种高效且准确的计算工具。

Abstract: This chapter discusses how a data-driven machine learning approach can reproduce key aspects of the physical behavior of multiphase flows in complex geological formations. We propose an end-to-end graph neural surrogate tailored to CO$_2$ plume migration forecasting in geological storage. The method is evaluated on the SPE11A benchmark, a well-known industry test case designed to assess CO$_2$ storage scenarios and characterized by sharp gas-water interfaces, strong advective transport, and rapid convective mixing with fingering development. The benchmark is reformulated as a graph in which nodes represent computational cells and edges encode transmissibility-based interactions enriched with geometric attributes. Directional transport arising from grid geometry, permeability contrasts, and geological heterogeneity is captured through an anisotropic message-passing mechanism, where interaction weights are computed via geometry-conditioned edge embeddings, biasing message aggregation toward physically relevant transport directions. Temporal evolution is modeled in latent space using an autoregressive residual formulation trained with multi-step supervision. The proposed model produces competitive forecasts of gas saturation and liquid-phase density, which are key indicators for CO$_2$ storage monitoring, with cumulative errors that remain moderate over extended forecasting horizons.

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems share state through memory stores, vector indices, and tool registries. The exclusion lattice over these anomalies is trivial; the contribution is the mechanically verified realizability and strict separation of one maximal chain within it, $L_0 \subsetneq \cdots \subsetneq L_4$, to our knowledge the first machine-checked consistency hierarchy for such runtimes. A development of 274 Verus obligations (zero assume, zero admit; trust base: two structural axioms and a mutex correspondence) proves the detectors sound and complete against the specifications and each runtime its avoidance set. Three deployed Rust runtimes realize L0-L1 (pessimistic locking, serializable snapshot isolation, default-SI), each verified against stale-generation and refined to its state machine; L2-L4 are exec-mode-verified with dependency-free prevention twins (A3, A6, A2: 0/1000 versus 1000/1000), and L2 is run live across three model families (A3 prevented in all 120 retracted sessions).   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出使用Finsler Laplacian作为Laplace-Beltrami算子的非线性替代方案，用于处理点云数据。
2. 证明了在点云样本数量增加时，离散化的Finsler Laplacian估计量能够收敛到流形上的真实算子。

Result: 理论上证明了离散估计的收敛性，并通过实验验证了Finslerian GNN能够有效还原非线性扩散方程底层的几何特征，优于传统的各向同性图神经网络架构。

Conclusion: 该研究通过在图神经网络中引入Finsler Laplacian，成功实现了对具有非线性几何结构数据的有效建模，克服了传统图拉普拉斯算子仅限于各向同性算子的局限性。该框架为捕捉流形上非线性扩散过程提供了理论基础和计算工具。

Abstract: Graph neural network architectures based on the graph Laplacian approximate the Laplace-Beltrami operator, thus limiting their application to isotropic operators. As a nonlinear alternative to the Laplace-Beltrami operator, we consider estimates of the Finsler Laplacian on point clouds sampled from a manifold. We prove that these discrete estimates converge to the true operator on the manifold as the number of point samples grows. Moreover, we show that this operator can be expressed as a graph neural network layer, which we use to define a family of Finslerian graph neural networks constrained to express Finsler geometry. We show that Finslerian graph neural networks recover the geometry underlying nonlinear diffusion equations in practice.

### [71] [Constrained Diffusion Models with Primal-Dual Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17192)
*Samar Hadou,Yigit Berkay Uslu,Alejandro Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于带约束熵正则化优化问题的原对偶扩散采样框架（PDI），通过在反向扩散过程中动态更新对偶变量并联合优化分布，实现了对约束条件的高效满足。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种名为原对偶推理（PDI）的方法：1. 在拉格朗日对偶域形式化约束采样问题，使其转化为吉布斯分布采样。2. 设计了一种双重条件化的评分网络，能够根据动态更新的对偶变量进行条件化去噪。3. 在反向扩散过程中，每一步先通过当前评分网络去噪，随后基于约束违反度对对偶变量执行梯度上升更新，实现两者的联合推理。

Result: 实验结果表明，PDI 在高斯混合模型采样、无线资源分配以及投资组合管理等任务中表现出色，能够有效地处理平均约束，生成的样本更符合约束条件，且在实际应用中展现了优于传统基准方法的性能。

Conclusion: 本文提出的原对偶推理（PDI）框架成功地将约束采样问题转化为原变量与对偶变量的联合优化，克服了传统方法中对偶变量预估计的缺陷。理论证明了该方法在收敛性上的有效性，并通过多领域实验验证了其在复杂约束环境下的鲁棒性与适用性。

Abstract: This paper develops constrained diffusion models with primal-dual inference (PDI) to sample from optimal distributions of entropy-regularized optimization problems with \emph{average} constraints. We formalize constrained sampling in the Lagrangian dual domain, where the optimal distribution takes the form of a Gibbs distribution indexed by the optimal dual variable. Rather than estimating this dual multiplier before sampling and freezing it throughout generation, PDI jointly infers the optimal primal distribution and its parametrizing dual variable. Each reverse diffusion step denoises using the score field associated with the current multiplier and then updates the multiplier through dual ascent using the estimated constraint violation of the denoised samples. To enable this conditional score field, we train a single dual-conditioned score network over the family of Gibbs distributions induced by the dual variables encountered during inference. We prove that the time average of the dual variables generated along the inference trajectory converges to a neighborhood of the dual optimum and bound the effect of residual dual mismatch on the terminal distribution through schedule-dependent stability factors. We evaluate PDI on constrained sampling from a mixture of Gaussians, wireless resource allocation, and portfolio management.

### [72] [PowerOPD: Stabilizing On-Policy Distillation with Bounded Power Transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17199)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准在线策略蒸馏（OPD）中的对数比奖励函数在实际训练中会导致严重的病态问题，如样本效率低、生成不稳定以及梯度方差极大，无法达到最优的蒸馏效果。

Method: 提出 PowerOPD 方法，利用 Box-Cox 幂变换将传统的无界对数比奖励转化为一组参数化（α > 0）的、具有符号一致性的有界奖励函数，从而有效控制梯度波动。

Result: PowerOPD 在六个数学推理基准测试和四个 Qwen3 师生模型对上表现优异，相比传统 OPD 平均得分提升最高达 6.37 分，同时节省了 59.2% 的计算时间及 23.1% 的显存占用，且梯度范数缩小了 3000 倍以上。

Abstract: Standard on-policy distillation (OPD) for large language models estimates the reverse-KL objective using student-sampled tokens, yielding an unbiased single-sample Monte Carlo estimator that avoids vocabulary-wide computation. However, we show that this estimator suffers from severe training pathologies in practice: sample inefficiency, unstable generation dynamics, and a substantial performance gap compared to exact full-vocabulary OPD. Reward-level diagnosis traces these pathologies to the log-ratio reward, which is unbounded by construction, producing extremely high-variance gradients concentrated at early positions and persisting throughout training; standard post-hoc scaling fail as they operate only after this distortion occurs. To solve this problem, we propose PowerOPD: a family of natively bounded, sign-consistent rewards from the Box-Cox power transformation, parameterized by alpha > 0, of which the log-ratio is the degenerate alpha -> 0 limit. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks and four Qwen3 teacher-student pairs, PowerOPD achieves benchmark-averaged Avg@8/Pass@8 gains of up to +6.37/+5.71 over vanilla OPD, +3.01/+3.54 over post-hoc stabilization, and +2.59/+8.90 over full-vocabulary OPD, while reducing wall-clock time by 59.2% and peak GPU memory by 23.1%. Larger alpha generally improves accuracy, consistently shortens responses, and keeps gradient norms more than 3,000x smaller than vanilla OPD.

### [73] [Sum-of-Squares Degree Barriers for the Reweighted-Hinge Method in Robust Halfspace Learning: A Christoffel-Function Characterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17215)
*Xiaoyu Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文分析了基于低阶矩的异常值剔除算法的局限性，证明了鲁棒学习中的噪声隐藏能力与数据分布的 Christoffel 函数紧密相关，并量化了 SoS 证书度数与算法容错性能之间的权衡边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的鲁棒学习方法通常通过低阶矩来剔除异常值，但这种方法存在盲点，即攻击者可以在低阶统计量无法感知的范围内隐藏噪声。本文旨在定量分析这种“盲点”的大小，探究 SoS 证书度数对异常值移除能力的限制，并解释为什么鲁棒学习的误差与度数之间存在特定的权衡关系。

Method: 本文将异常值移除问题转化为一种反转视角，利用 Sum-of-Squares (SoS) 证明理论，将攻击者隐藏噪声的能力与清洁边际分布的 Christoffel 函数 $λ_{t+1}(c)$ 联系起来。通过重加权铰链（reweighted-hinge）方法，分析了在不同 SoS 度数下异常值对学习半空间模型的影响，并构建了对应的度数-边界权衡模型与 barrier 实例。

Result: 1. 确定了对于 degree-$2t$ 证书，隐藏噪声的极限为 Christoffel 函数 $λ_{t+1}(c)$；2. 推导出了边际-度数权衡：将 $ε$ 误差降至目标水平所需的 SoS 度数为 $Ω(\log(1/ε))$；3. 发现了度数-$2$ 的“屏障”（barrier），即存在某些情况，仅凭 $2$ 阶矩无法突破 $η^{1/2}$ 的错误率，而更高阶矩（如度数 $4$）则可以改善；4. 证明了度数-$2t$ 算法可达到的鲁棒性前沿为 $η^{1-1/2t}$。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了基于低阶矩的异常值检测证书存在本质的“盲区”，该盲区由清洁数据的 Christoffel 函数决定。研究明确了 Sum-of-Squares (SoS) 证书的度数与鲁棒学习中的容错能力之间存在权衡关系，证明了现有算法在特定度数下的最优性与局限性，为理解鲁棒学习的复杂性提供了理论基础。

Abstract: A certificate that removes outliers sees the data only through its low-degree moments, and an adversary exploits exactly this, hiding corruption where the clean data already looks typical, in the blind spot no bounded-degree test resolves. That blind spot turns out to have an exact size: the Christoffel function of the clean marginal, the very quantity modern data analysis thresholds to detect outliers, here read from the adversary's side as the corruption a bounded-degree certificate cannot remove. We turn this inversion into the organizing principle of the reweighted-hinge approach to robustly learning $γ$-margin halfspaces under malicious noise (Shen, 2025; Zeng and Shen, 2025): the governing resource is the Sum-of-Squares degree of the outlier-removal certificate, and the resolution principle states that the maximal corruption mass which can hide at a center $c$ from a degree-$2t$ certificate is exactly the Christoffel function $λ_{t+1}(c)$ of the clean marginal. Three consequences follow, all against the certificate method (not information-theoretic). A margin-degree tradeoff: certifying the dense pancake to error $ε$ costs SoS degree $Ω(\log(1/ε))$ or margin $Ω(\sqrt{\log(1/ε)}/\sqrt{d})$, explaining why the $\log(1/ε)$ margin Shen (2025) records is forced, with a weighted-Chebyshev reduction making the threshold $2t=Θ((|c|/s)^2)$ tight modulo one classical weighted-extremal estimate. A degree-$2$ outlier barrier: the resolution principle realized as an explicit instance on which degree $2$ is stuck at $η^{1/2}$ while degree $4$ escapes, locating the method's small breakdown rate in the degree, not the analysis. And a degree-$2t$ algorithm tracing the frontier $η^{1-1/2t}$ (recovering Shen (2025) at $t=1$), whose gain is an explicit constant, capped by the pancake density and shown unimprovable by the degree-$2$ barrier.
