### [165] [Incumbent Advantage: Brand Bias and Cognitive Manipulation Dynamics in LLM Recommendation Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17443)
*Xi Chu,Yupeng Hou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型推荐系统中的品牌竞争动态，揭示了知名品牌优势的脆弱性、营销话术对模型决策的干预能力，以及盲目追求生成式引擎优化（GEO）可能导致的市场收益恶化（社会困境）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）逐渐成为消费者发现产品的主要渠道，目前尚不清楚品牌如何在这一新媒介中进行竞争。研究旨在探讨LLM推荐系统中的品牌动态，以及生成式引擎优化（GEO）作为营销手段对市场竞争格局的影响。

Method: 研究采用实验法，在护肤品类别下对三个主流商用LLM（GPT-4o-mini, Claude Sonnet, Gemini 3 Flash）进行了三项实验：1. 测试在产品规格相同时品牌知名度的影响；2. 引入权威营销话术（包括虚假临床声明）以观察其对模型推荐偏好的影响；3. 构建多品牌GEO竞争模型，评估不同优化策略下的收益变化。

Result: 1. 存在“条件垄断”现象，知名品牌在产品规格一致时具有绝对推荐优势，但这种优势极易被竞争对手微小的评分领先打破；2. 权威风格的营销话术（即便包含伪造的临床证据）能有效打破垄断，且不同模型对该策略的响应程度不同；3. 多品牌间的GEO竞争导致“社会困境”，当所有品牌均采用优化策略时，个体收益大幅下滑，而不参与优化策略的品牌则完全无法获得推荐。

Conclusion: 生成式引擎优化（GEO）不仅是安全问题，更是一种塑造市场竞争的新兴营销实践。品牌在LLM生态中的竞争呈现出高度的敏感性和不稳定性，企业若盲目跟随GEO策略可能陷入“社会困境”，导致收益急剧下降。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are becoming a major way for consumers to find products, but we do not yet understand how brands compete in this new channel. We study brand dynamics in LLM recommendations using skincare products -- a category where consumers cannot easily judge quality before buying and must rely on brand reputation -- across three commercial LLMs (GPT-4o-mini, Claude Sonnet, Gemini 3 Flash), with a robustness check on search goods. In three experiments, we find: (1) a Conditional Monopoly where well-known brands get recommended 100% of the time (IAI = 10.0) when all products have the same specifications, but this dominance disappears with less than a +0.1-star rating advantage for a competitor; (2) authority-style marketing language, including fabricated clinical-evidence claims, breaks this monopoly at a Bias Surplus Value equal to +0.17 rating points, with each model responding differently; and (3) a social dilemma in multi-brand GEO competition: when all brands adopt the same optimization strategy, individual payoff falls from +0.802 to +0.007 in our payoff proxy, and non-participating brands receive zero recommendations in our tests. Our results suggest that generative engine optimization (GEO) should be studied not only as a security risk, but also as an emerging marketing practice that shapes market competition.

### [166] [A Machine-Learned Comorbidity Index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17450)
*Suleman Baloch,Kishlay Jha,Alberto M. Segre,Philip M. Polgreen,Bijaya Adhikari*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种机器学习共病指数（MLCI），通过优化nHSIC来捕捉诊断代码与多种临床结局之间的复杂非线性关系，解决了传统评分系统（如Charlson）过于单一且缺乏灵活性的问题，在多个EHR数据集上表现出优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的共病评分（如Charlson和Elixhauser指数）存在两大局限性：一是其过于关注死亡率，无法很好地匹配其他临床结局；二是其基于线性规则的结构，难以捕捉复杂的非线性风险关系。为此，研究旨在开发一种能适应多种临床结局并具备非线性建模能力的共病评估方法。

Method: 提出了一种机器学习共病指数（MLCI）模型。该方法通过最大化归一化希尔伯特-施密特独立性准则（nHSIC），将诊断编码映射为单一标量，从而捕捉诊断与多种临床结局之间的非线性风险依赖关系。此外，研究还提供了理论支持，以表征在不同临床结局间实现统一且信息丰富的入院级别排序的条件。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用机器学习方法构建的共病指数（MLCI）能够突破传统线性规则的局限，提供一种更灵活、更准确的患者风险评估方式，且在多种临床结局预测中具有通用性。

Abstract: Traditional comorbidity scores (e.g., Charlson and Elixhauser) are widely used for risk adjustment and patient stratification, but they have two key limitations: (i) they are largely mortality-centric and do not align well with other clinical outcomes, and (ii) their linear, rule-based structure cannot capture nonlinear, outcome-specific risk relationships. We propose a Machine-Learned Comorbidity Index (MLCI) that maps diagnosis codes to a single scalar by maximizing the normalized Hilbert-Schmidt Independence Criterion (nHSIC) between the learned score and multiple clinical outcomes. MLCI captures nonlinear risk-outcome dependence and is supported by a theory that characterizes when a unified, informative admission-level ordering can be achieved across outcomes. Empirical results on multiple benchmark electronic health record (EHR) datasets show that MLCI outperforms strong baselines across multiple evaluation metrics.

</details>


### [167] [MapSatisfyBench: Benchmarking Satisfaction-Aware Map Agents through Behavior-Grounded Implicit Decision Factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17453)
*Lubin Bai,Mengyu Cao,Sixue Wang,Zhongwei Wan,Yue Pan,Jiale Hou,Xiang Li,Xiuyuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对地图智能体在处理用户隐性需求时的不足，本文提出了一个评估框架 MapSatisfyBench，旨在推动地图智能体从单纯的任务完成转向主动识别并满足用户隐性决策因素的满意度导向决策模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在地图服务等日常场景中，用户查询往往是不完整的，包含许多未明说的“隐性决策因素”。现有的地图智能体主要关注明确的任务完成，缺乏对这些隐性因素的识别和主动恢复能力，且目前缺乏评估这种能力的有效基准。

Method: 提出了“恢复-识别-过滤（restore-identify-filter）”框架，从用户行为链证据中重构完整的用户需求，识别出其中的隐性决策因素，并仅保留有预查询证据支持的因素；基于此构建了 MapSatisfyBench 基准数据集，包含五个维度的标注，实现了对地图智能体满意度感知能力的全面评估。

Result: 实验表明，当前的主流智能体在处理显性任务方面表现出色，但在处理隐性决策因素和主动获取满意度相关决策证据方面能力受限。MapSatisfyBench 为后续研究提供了一个客观、可量化的评估框架。

Conclusion: 现有的地图智能体虽然能较好地完成明确的任务，但在识别和满足用户的隐性决策因素方面仍存在不足。MapSatisfyBench 的提出标志着地图智能体的评价标准从单一的“任务完成度”向更深层次的“用户满意度导向的决策能力”转型。

Abstract: Large language model agents are increasingly integrated into map services. Since map services are embedded in everyday-life scenarios rather than professional task settings, users often express their needs informally, resulting in underspecified queries with many unspoken needs, namely, implicit decision factors that are critical for user satisfaction. Although clarification is an effective way to mitigate this issue, it increases user burden in daily interaction, and a capable agent should first proactively recover such factors from available information sources. However, evaluating this ability is challenging. The first challenge is to determine which implicit decision factors are suitable for evaluation. A factor is evaluable only if it affects user acceptance and can be recovered from information available to the agent before it responds. Second, user satisfaction cannot be reliably represented by a single reference answer, requiring a benchmark that converts satisfaction-relevant factors into objective and quantifiable evaluation targets. To address these challenges, we propose a restore-identify-filter framework that reconstructs complete user needs from behavior-chain evidence, identifies implicit decision factors, and retains only those supported by pre-query evidence. Building on this methodology, we construct MapSatisfyBench from large-scale, real-world anonymized user data and annotate ground truth from five dimensions and enables full-chain evaluation of satisfaction-aware map agents. Experiments show that current agents generally perform well on explicit task completion, but remain limited in satisfying implicit decision factors and proactively acquiring the evidence needed for satisfaction-aware decisions. These findings establish MapSatisfyBench as a benchmark for shifting map-agent evaluation from task completion toward satisfaction-aware spatial decision making.

### [168] [Dissecting model behavior through agent trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17454)
*Gaurav Gupta,Vatshank Chaturvedi,Jun Huan,Anoop Deoras*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出AI代理的性能很大程度上取决于系统执行框架，并定义了“意图-执行”差距。作者开发了SSA框架，不仅在多项基准测试中达到了顶尖水平，还通过大规模轨迹分析揭示了不同模型在解决问题时的底层行为模式差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的AI代理研究过度关注模型本身的建模能力，而忽视了代理系统（harness）与模型假设之间的不匹配问题。作者认为，这种“意图-执行”差距直接制约了模型潜力的发挥，因此需要一套能够实现模型与执行环境高效对齐的方法论，并超越简单的pass@1指标来理解代理的真实行为模式。

Method: 1. 提出“意图-执行”差距的概念，主张通过系统性的对齐来弥合模型与执行器（harness）之间的差异。
2. 开发了简单且可定制的代理框架“Simple Strands Agent (SSA)”，该框架旨在捕捉跨模型家族的通用模式及特定的模型偏好。
3. 利用SSA在SWE-Pro、SWE-Verified和Terminal-Bench-2等基准测试上进行性能评估。
4. 对138k条代理轨迹进行代码状态空间分析，通过编辑频率、测试活动和阶段转换等细粒度指标评估模型的解决问题行为。

Result: 1. 成功在多个主流代理基准测试（SWE-Pro、SWE-Verified和Terminal-Bench-2）中复现或超越了各大模型厂商报告的pass@1性能。
2. 通过对138k条轨迹的深入分析，发现即便在pass@1指标相似的情况下，不同模型在解决问题时的策略（如编辑频率、测试行为和阶段转换）存在显著差异，证明了细粒度分析对于理解代理行为至关重要。

Conclusion: 本文强调了人工智能代理的性能不仅仅取决于模型能力，更是一个系统工程问题。通过缩小“意图-执行”差距（intent-execution gap），即模型预期与系统执行之间的不匹配，可以显著提升代理的实际表现。此外，通过代码状态空间分析，研究揭示了不同模型在解决问题时的行为差异和策略偏好，为评估代理能力提供了比单纯的pass@1指标更深入的维度。

Abstract: AI agent performance is not just a modeling problem, it is fundamentally a systems problem. The advanced capabilities of models are realized through agent harnesses. Therefore, a gap between model assumptions and harness behavior can easily prevent the model's full capabilities from translating into agent performance. We formalize this as the `intent-execution' gap: the mismatch between what the model intends and what the harness executes, and vice versa. We argue that minimizing this intent-execution gap is as important as other aspects of harness design such as tools and execution loops. To illustrate the impact of this harness-model alignment, we develop a simple and customizable harness called `Simple Strands Agent' (SSA). SSA aims to find the bulk of common patterns which generalize across different model families (such as Claude, Gemini, GPT, Grok, Qwen), as well as a small number of model-specific preferences. We make two contributions: (i) we $\textbf{reproduce or improve on the pass@1}$ performance reported by diverse model-provider families on popular agentic benchmarks (SWE-Pro, SWE-Verified and Terminal-Bench-2), and (ii) building on an $\textbf{analysis of 138k trajectories generated by SSA}$, we look beyond the $\texttt{pass@1}$ numbers which tend to be relatively even across frontier models. By representing agent trajectories in code state-spaces, we observe model-level differences in problem-solving behavior. Finer-grained metrics such as edit frequency, testing activity, and phase-transitions reveal how individual models allocate effort across different stages of autonomous problem solving.

</details>


### [169] [Can LLMs Be CEOs? Benchmarking Strategic Resource Reallocation with Multi-Role Agent Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17459)
*Yuyang Dai,Xueqing Peng,Lingfei Qian,Zhuohan Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CEO-Bench基准，旨在评估大模型在高管层面的战略资源分配决策能力，发现模型在应对复杂、冲突性的组织决策时，虽然能输出合规计划，但在策略敏锐度、历史关联和大胆决策上仍有待突破。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型评估基准多集中于孤立的认知任务（如推理、知识检索），忽略了真实高管决策的核心挑战：即在复杂的组织约束下，整合利益相关者提供的冲突性建议，并进行战略资源分配。

Method: 构建了一个名为CEO-Bench的多智能体基准测试。该基准模拟了包含信息不对称、组织约束和时间依赖的多轮战略资源重新分配场景。模型需综合来自四位具有不同优先级和私有信息的C级高管（CFO、CTO、COO、CMO）的冲突建议，并从角色整合、条件大胆度、历史敏感性及计划有效性四个维度进行评估。

Result: 实验发现，五个前沿模型在计划的结构有效性上表现良好，但在“战略校准”方面存在显著差异。研究识别出三大系统性故障模式：单一顾问偏见（单方捕获）、模糊环境下的保守倾向、以及历史记忆缺失。此外，模型在深度整合冲突意见与做出果断决策之间存在明显的权衡。

Conclusion: 当前大模型在执行层面的决策能力存在显著瓶颈，尤其是在处理冲突建议与大胆决策之间的权衡上。研究结果揭示了模型在真实商业决策场景下的局限性，并为未来构建AI辅助的高管决策系统提供了关键的设计参考。

Abstract: Evaluating the decision-making capabilities of large language models (LLMs) is a growing research priority, yet existing benchmarks focus on isolated cognitive tasks such as reasoning, knowledge retrieval, and economic rationality in stylized settings. These evaluations overlook the defining challenge of real executive decision-making: integrating conflicting recommendations from specialized stakeholders under information asymmetry, organizational constraints, and temporal dependencies. We introduce \textsc{CEO-Bench}, a multi-agent benchmark that evaluates LLMs on CEO-level strategic resource reallocation -- the process of redirecting capital across business units in a multi-round, constraint-rich organizational environment. In \textsc{CEO-Bench}, LLM agents receive conflicting advice from four role-conditioned C-suite advisors (CFO, CTO, COO, CMO), each with private signals and distinct priorities, and must synthesize these into a concrete allocation plan evaluated along four dimensions: role integration, conditional boldness, history-sensitive judgment, and plan validity. Experiments across five frontier models on 13 scenarios reveal that all models achieve high structural validity but diverge sharply on strategic calibration -- the hardest capability layer. We identify systematic failure modes including single-advisor capture, conservative default under ambiguity, and historical amnesia, and uncover a structural integration-boldness tradeoff: models that engage more deeply with conflicting perspectives tend to produce less decisive action. These findings delineate the current capability boundary of LLMs as organizational decision-makers and inform the design of future AI-assisted executive systems.

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于课程内容的LLM评估流水线不仅证明了在教育评估中引入大模型的潜力，还强调了通过结构化、可验证的流程将AI判定与官方教学大纲及评分标准挂钩的重要性。该系统为教育领域应用生成式AI提供了可信的实现范式。

Abstract: Generative AI and large language models (LLMs) are increasingly applied to question generation and automated assessment. This paper presents a curriculum-grounded, configurable LLM-as-Judge pipeline for question-level marking, co-developed with an industrial partner, to support exam preparation for university admission. The pipeline identifies the relevant topics, subtopics, and cognitive demand of a question, and assembles verifiable and authorised context to support LLM judgement. Curriculum intent is operationalised through concrete syllabus artefacts, including prescribed verbs and outcomes, performance band descriptors, glossary definitions, and marking-guideline principles. A staged LLM workflow is employed to first generate question-specific rubrics, capturing structured expectations of performance, and then derive and evaluate marking criteria used to allocate marks to student responses. This design improves consistency, transparency, and alignment with official marking practices. Preliminary evaluation shows that the proposed LLM-as-Judge pipeline delivers marking outcomes comparable to human tutors, while yielding justifications that are more traceable to authorised curriculum artefacts and marking standards. The pipeline has also been integrated into an online study platform, where early deployment data provide initial insights into operational usage and manual overrides.

### [171] [SEAGym: An Evaluation Environment for Self-Evolving LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17546)
*Congjie Zheng,Chuanyi Xue,Bin Liang,Jun Yang,Changshui Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SEAGym 评估环境，用于系统性分析自进化 LLM 智能体架构（Agent Harness）的更新过程，揭示了单纯的性能指标难以捕捉架构进化中存在的过拟合、能力倒退和成本失控等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的自进化 LLM 智能体主要通过改进“架构套件”（Agent Harness，包括提示词、记忆、工具等）来提升性能，但现有的评估方法过于单一，难以区分架构更新是产生了可复用的改进、过拟合了近期任务、增加了成本，还是损害了旧有能力。

Method: 提出了一个名为 SEAGym 的评估环境，旨在衡量智能体架构更新的全生命周期。它将 Harbor 兼容的基准测试转化为动态的任务源，包括训练批次、冻结更新验证、ID（分布内）与 OOD（分布外）迁移视图、重放诊断以及快照和指标记录，实现了对进化过程的全面追踪。

Result: 在 Terminal-Bench 2.0 和 HLE 上的实验表明，ACE、TF-GRPO 和 AHE 等方法在 SEAGym 下表现出不同的进化动力学。结果显示：频繁更新可能导致无法提升保留测试集的性能；有用的中间快照可能会在后续进化中“坍塌”；同时，任务源的多样性和底层模型的选择对架构的稳定性有重要影响。

Conclusion: SEAGym 提供了一套多维度的评估视角，证明了对智能体架构（Agent Harness）的频繁更新并不等同于性能的稳步提升。研究强调了在智能体自我进化过程中，平衡通用性、稳健性和成本效益的重要性，并指出模型后端和任务多样性对架构可靠性有显著影响。

Abstract: Self-evolving LLM-based agents improve mainly by changing their agent harness: the structured execution layer around a base model, including prompts, memory, tools, middleware, runtime state, and the model-tool interaction loop. Existing evaluations often reduce this process to isolated task scores or a single sequential curve, obscuring whether an update produces reusable improvement, overfits recent tasks, increases cost, or harms older behavior. We introduce SEAGym, an evaluation environment for measuring agent harness updates across training, validation, test, replay, and cost records. SEAGym turns Harbor-compatible benchmarks into dynamic self-evolution task sources with train batches, frozen update-validation, held-out ID and OOD transfer views, replay diagnostics, and saved snapshot and metric records. Instantiating SEAGym on Terminal-Bench 2.0 and HLE, we compare ACE, TF-GRPO, and AHE under a shared epoch/batch protocol. The results show that these evaluation views provide complementary signals about the evolution process: frequent updates may fail to improve held-out performance, useful intermediate snapshots may collapse later, and source diversity and model backend can affect harness reliability.

</details>


### [172] [DeepInsight: A Unified Evaluation Infrastructure Across the Physical AI Stack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17574)
*Siyi Li,Chunyu Sun,Jiahao Zhang,Yuchen Kang,Wuliang Wang,Yu Qiu,Rui Jiang,Haitao Cui,Jie Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DeepInsight 是一种针对物理 AI 栈设计的全栈评估基础设施，通过统一的抽象接口和共享的追踪系统，解决了大模型与物理控制层级之间评估割裂的问题，实现了高效的跨层级故障诊断与性能分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的物理 AI 栈（从大模型解码到物理控制）跨度极大，现有的评估方式被迫将不同层级拼接在一起，导致运行时与评分机制互不兼容，无法进行跨层级的回归诊断，难以捕捉不同层级交互产生的复杂问题。

Method: 提出了 DeepInsight 评估基础设施，通过引入三个核心抽象（任务 Task、资源 Resource、结果 Result）实现跨层级统一。其关键创新包括：1. 统一的场景驱动程序；2. 适用于所有后端（LLM 推理及物理沙箱）的资源处理协议；3. 全局共享的追踪身份方案，确保所有层级的事件记录在同一时间线上。

Result: 在生产环境中成功部署于具身人形机器人全栈；在大模型推理端，其性能与现有主流基准测试一致，且具备更快的单节点执行速度和近线性的多节点扩展能力；最重要的是实现了跨层级诊断，能精准定位从一层引发并在另一层显现的问题。

Conclusion: DeepInsight 通过在单一运行时中统一物理 AI 栈的评估，克服了现有割裂式评估框架无法进行跨层诊断的局限。该系统证明了在异构资源（从大模型推理到物理控制）中应用统一抽象的可行性，为具身智能系统的稳健开发提供了有效的全栈评估路径。

Abstract: Evaluating a Physical AI stack spans operators that differ by more than three orders of magnitude -- from a single foundation-model decoding step to thousands of physics ticks of whole-body control -- varying orthogonally in modality, reward semantics, and resource profile. No existing framework spans this range, so the stack is evaluated today by stitching together separate harnesses that share neither runtime nor scoring, preserving each segment's local validity but losing the shared identity needed to diagnose cross-layer regressions. We present DeepInsight, an evaluation infrastructure that serves this full spectrum on a single runtime. Rather than homogenize the regimes, it preserves their heterogeneity behind three narrow abstractions -- task, resource, and result -- each realized as one invariant shared by every subsystem: one episode driver, one resource-handle protocol implemented by every expensive backend (LLM inference and sandboxed runtimes alike), and one trace identity scheme under which every event is written. Deployed in production across all three layers of an embodied humanoid stack, this single set of invariants onboards new benchmarks largely by configuration. Where mature peer orchestrators exist -- at the foundation-model end -- it reproduces published references and peer-framework readings within their own spread, runs the same suites faster on a single node, and scales near-linearly across nodes. Its distinctive return is diagnostic: because every layer writes into one shared trace, a regression that begins in one layer and surfaces in another stays localizable on that trace -- a cross-layer payoff no federation of per-segment harnesses can reproduce.

</details>


### [173] [Surrogate Assisted Pedestrian Protection Design via a Foundation Model Orchestrated Workflow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17577)
*Osamu Ito,Akihiko Katagiri,Yoshikazu Nakagawa,Shin Saeki,Jun Shiraishi,Masato Sasaki*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种首创的基础模型驱动工作流，通过集成代理模型、多目标优化、几何变形和多模态大模型交互，将汽车碰撞安全设计的评估时间缩短至秒级，并能快速生成多种符合标准的设计方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在工程领域，碰撞安全设计因涉及高度非线性的接触动力学、材料非线性和离散状态转换，传统数据驱动的代理模型难以准确建模。研究旨在克服这些挑战，通过引入基础模型驱动的工作流，加速碰撞安全设计过程。

Method: 该研究提出了一种由基础模型驱动的碰撞安全设计工作流，包含四个核心组件：1) 基于CAE仿真数据训练的代理模型，用于预测行人腿部损伤指标并提供预测区间；2) 使用NSGA-II算法进行多目标演化搜索；3) 利用基于变形的几何生成器实现参数到3D拓扑结构的映射；4) 构建包含大语言模型(LLM)和视觉-语言模型的自然语言交互界面，用于任务调度与设计语义比较。

Result: 在汽车前保险杠的案例研究中，该工作流成功将单次评估时间从传统的数小时缩短至数秒。在单次探索中生成了35种符合安全标准的设计方案，显著缩短了传统CAE迭代所需的数周时间，且代理模型的平均预测准确度（R²）达到0.87。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了基础模型可以作为机器学习代理模型与物理仿真之间的集成层，有效提升安全关键工程领域（如汽车碰撞安全设计）的研发效率，推动AI在复杂工程任务中的应用。

Abstract: AI-driven engineering workflows face particular challenges in crash safety design: unlike aerodynamics, crash events involve highly nonlinear contact dynamics, material nonlinearity, and discrete state transitions that are difficult to capture with data-driven surrogate models. To the best of our knowledge, we present the first foundation model--orchestrated workflow for crash safety design that enables surrogate-assisted exploration for pedestrian protection, reducing evaluation time from hours per CAE simulation to seconds.
  The workflow integrates four components: (1) a surrogate trained on CAE crash simulations to predict pedestrian leg injury metrics from design parameters, achieving an average $R^2=0.87$ and providing distribution-free conformal prediction intervals; (2) multiobjective evolutionary search (NSGA-II) to discover diverse feasible parameter sets under user-specified constraints; (3) a morphing-based geometry generator that maps parameters to topology-preserving 3D shapes; and (4) a natural-language interface in which an LLM orchestrates the workflow and a vision--language model supports semantic comparison of generated designs.
  In an automotive front-bumper case study, the workflow produces 35 distinct safety-compliant alternatives from a single exploration, a process that would require weeks with conventional CAE iteration. These results suggest that foundation models can serve as integration layers between ML surrogates and physics-based simulation, helping bring AI capabilities to safety-critical engineering domains.

</details>


### [174] [Closing the Feedback Loop: From Experience Extraction to Insight Governance in Verbal Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17591)
*Yanwei Cui,Xing Zhang,Yulong Zhang,Li Shao,Xiaofeng Shi,Guanghui Wang,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文针对免训练大模型智能体在非平稳环境中的知识积累问题，提出了一种包含规则、证据和技能的三层治理架构，通过闭环的策展机制平衡了经验的保留与遗忘，显著提升了模型在动态环境下的适应能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 免训练的基于语言的强化学习允许智能体通过环境反馈改进行为，但在非平稳环境下，智能体陷入了“保留-遗忘”的困境：保留旧经验会导致负面迁移，而完全丢弃则会导致灾难性遗忘。现有研究过于关注经验提取而忽视了对知识的治理，该论文旨在解决这一治理缺口。

Method: 提出了一种“规则（Rules）-证据（Evidence）-技能（Skills）”三层治理架构。该方法通过一个反馈驱动的策展循环（curation loop）进行管理：规则用于提取经验，证据日志用于跟踪规则的可靠性，技能层则负责决策应用、冲突解决及适时止损。这一机制将非参数化的动态治理引入大模型，实现了对知识生命周期的精细化控制。

Result: 以金融预测为案例研究，实验结果表明，在存在反馈策展循环的情况下，智能体能够显著提升预测准确性和风险调整后收益；而在缺乏治理的情况下，累积的经验反而会导致模型性能下降至零样本基准以下。这证明了该架构在处理嘈杂、非平稳环境反馈方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出了一种三层治理架构，有效解决了非平稳环境中免训练强化学习面临的“保留-遗忘”困境。通过引入经验管理机制，不仅避免了陈旧知识带来的负面迁移，也防止了灾难性遗忘，从而使大模型智能体能够真正从反馈中持续进化，在金融预测等复杂场景中表现出色。

Abstract: Training-free verbal reinforcement learning enables LLM agents to learn from world feedback -- objective signals such as dynamic task outcomes, market returns, or demand forecasts -- by extracting verbal rules from experience and injecting them as context, updating the agent's behavior without parameter changes. However, in non-stationary environments these agents face a retention-forgetting dilemma: retaining stale insights causes negative transfer, while discarding them causes catastrophic forgetting when conditions recur. We identify four requirements for navigating this dilemma -- outcome-driven evaluation, persistent structured evidence, non-monotonic knowledge lifecycle, and compositional governance -- and show that existing methods invest heavily in experience extraction while underinvesting in insight governance. We propose a three-layer architecture -- rules, evidence, and skills -- connected by a feedback-driven curation loop that closes the governance gap. Rules capture distilled experience from world outcomes; evidence logs track each rule's reliability across episodes; skills govern which rules to apply, how to resolve conflicts, and when to abstain. On financial forecasting as a case study, where world feedback is naturally abundant, noisy, and non-stationary, we show that the same accumulated experience either degrades performance below the zero-shot baseline or dramatically improves accuracy and risk-adjusted returns, depending on whether the curation loop is present.

</details>


### [175] [Brick-DICL: Dynamic In-Context Learning for Automated Brick Schema Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17637)
*Yiyue Qian,Shinan Zhang,Huan Song,Negin Sokhandan,Hannah Marlowe,Diego Socolinsky*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“Brick-DICL”的两阶段动态上下文学习框架。其核心组件包括：1. Metadata-RAG，通过检索相关示例增强 LLM 对建筑领域知识的理解；2. Class-RAG，用于缩小分类空间，克服 Brick 本体类别过多的问题；3. 多 LLM 过滤机制，通过交叉验证识别低置信度结果，减少人工干预。

Abstract: Building Management Systems (BMS) are essential for optimizing energy efficiency and operational performance in modern buildings. However, the lack of standardization across BMS points from different manufacturers creates significant barriers to integration and data utilization. While the Brick schema offers a standardized ontology for building systems, mapping BMS points to appropriate Brick classes presents three critical challenges: (i) the extensive number of Brick classes (936 in the latest version), (ii) limited domain-specific knowledge in large language models (LLMs), and (iii) substantial manual effort required for verification. To address these challenges, we propose Brick-DICL, a two-stage dynamic in-context learning framework for automated Brick schema classification. Brick-DICL consists of two primary components: metadata-RAG, which retrieves relevant examples to enhance LLMs' domain knowledge, and class-RAG, which narrows down potential Brick classes to address the large classification space. Additionally, we implement a multi-LLM filtering mechanism that compares predictions across multiple models, flagging low-confidence classifications for human review. As a result: (i) General: Brick-DICL is applicable to any building management system regardless of manufacturer or metadata format; (ii) Novel and Powerful: as the first dynamic in-context learning approach for Brick schema classification, Brick-DICL achieves significant classification accuracy improvements on building datasets, outperforming existing methods; (iii) Efficient: our multi-LLM filtering strategy reduces manual verification effort, enabling rapid digital building onboarding. Extensive experiments demonstrate Brick-DICL's effectiveness across diverse building datasets, accelerating the path toward standardized, interoperable building management systems.

### [176] [FinAcumen: Financial Multimodal Reasoning via Self-Evolving Experience Memory Harness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17642)
*Pianran Guo,Pengcheng Zhou,Yucheng Jian,Shuhua Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FinAcumen 是一个为金融多模态推理设计的智能体框架，通过建立具备“经验总结”功能的持久化记忆库，让模型能够从过往的成功和失败中学习，从而大幅降低了金融分析中的推理幻觉并提升了决策准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了 FinAcumen 框架，核心在于构建一个基于“选择性经验记忆”的存储库。该方法包括：1. 自动从历史轨迹中提炼成功策略与失败预警规则；2. 在推理阶段，根据语义相关度阈值动态检索并应用经验；3. 引入回退机制以抑制不相关信息的干扰；4. 配合确定的金融工具环境（数值计算、检索、视觉解码、结果校验）进行多模态推理。

Conclusion: FinAcumen 通过引入选择性经验记忆机制，显著提升了金融领域多模态推理的可靠性和准确性。该研究证明了利用历史推理经验（包括成功策略与失败教训）来引导模型推理，是解决当前大模型在金融复杂任务中幻觉和推理不稳问题的有效途径。

Abstract: Financial multimodal reasoning requires agents to coordinate numerical computation, retrieval, visual interpretation, and temporal grounding across heterogeneous evidence sources. Existing tool-augmented agents improve execution fidelity, yet remain largely stateless across episodes, repeatedly rediscovering reasoning strategies and failure patterns. In high-stakes financial settings, this leads to unreliable tool routing, noisy retrieval, and hallucination-prone reasoning. We present FinAcumen, a financial reasoning agent framework centered on selective experience memory for tool-augmented multimodal reasoning. FinAcumen accumulates financially grounded reasoning experience from prior trajectories, distilling successful strategies and failure-derived cautionary rules into a persistent memory bank. During inference, retrieved experiences condition reasoning only when semantic relevance exceeds a calibrated threshold, while irrelevant memory is explicitly suppressed through a fallback mechanism. A deterministic financial tool environment further grounds numerical computation, retrieval, visual decoding, and answer verification.Across four financial multimodal reasoning benchmarks, FinAcumen consistently improves a frozen 8B vision-language model over finance-specialized models and approaches leading proprietary general-purpose models. Further analysis shows that selective experience activation improves reasoning reliability under retrieval uncertainty. Our code is anonymously available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/FinAcumen

### [177] [Beyond Domains: Reusing Web Skills via Transferable Interaction Patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17645)
*Shiqi He,Yue Cui,Feijie Wu,Xinyu Ma,Jiaheng Lu,Yaliang Li,Bolin Ding,Mosharaf Chowdhury*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillMigrator 是一种能够跨网站复用交互技能的网页智能体，通过匹配页面布局结构而非特定元素，显著降低了 LLM 调用成本并缩短了任务执行序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 网页智能体通常将动作分解为底层的原始操作，导致在复杂任务中执行路径过长，从而增加了 LLM 的推理成本和延迟。虽然现有的“网页技能”方法可以简化操作序列，但由于依赖于指令相似度或粗糙的元数据，导致在陌生网站上的复用率极低，无法充分发挥减少交互步数和 Token 消耗的潜力。

Method: 本文提出了 SkillMigrator 框架。该框架将成功轨迹中总结的交互模式存储为“可迁移交互模式”（TIP），其中包含技能本身及其诱导时的页面结构草图。在测试阶段，智能体通过计算目标页面的布局相似度来检索最优 TIP，并将技能逻辑映射到当前页面元素上。这种方法摆脱了对特定元素引用的依赖，实现了跨网站的技能复用。

Result: 实验结果表明，与现有的主流方法相比，SkillMigrator 在保持相同成功率的前提下，在 WebArena 和 Mind2Web 基准测试中成功轨迹的平均 LLM 动作数减少了 8% 至 10%。

Conclusion: SkillMigrator 通过基于页面布局结构的技能迁移机制，有效地提升了网页智能体的执行效率。该研究证明了利用结构相似性而非传统指令或元数据匹配来实现技能复用，能够显著减少 LLM 的调用次数，为构建更高效、更具泛化能力的网页智能体提供了新路径。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) web agents are usually deployed as tool callers: each turn, the model reads a fresh page observation and emits one structured tool action. When every action is a low-level primitive, horizons grow quickly and so do policy-facing LLM completions, dominating latency and cost on benchmarks such as Mind2Web and WebArena. Recent systems therefore wrap repeated interaction fragments as web skills: callable tools built from successful trajectories or induced programs, so one call can replace several primitives. However, prior skill libraries are still triggered mainly by instruction similarity or coarse site metadata, which yields low skill reuse on held-out sites and leaves much of the potential step and token reduction on the table.
  We present SkillMigrator, an agent that learns reusable web skills and transfers them across sites by matching layout structure rather than specific element references. Each induced skill is stored as a transferable interaction pattern (TIP): the skill paired with a structural sketch of the snapshot at induction time. At test time, SkillMigrator retrieves TIPs by layout similarity and grounds their references on the live page. The rest of the stack is standard: accessibility-snapshot observations with stable references, and fixed tool calling over primitives plus skill invocations. Compared with the state-of-the-art approaches, SkillMigrator reduces the average LLM-action count on successful trajectories by 8-10% across both WebArena and Mind2Web at matched success rate.

### [178] [From Brewing to Resolution: Tracing the Internal Lifecycle of Code Reasoning in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17648)
*Siyue Chen,Yifu Guo,Yuquan Lu,Zishan Xu,Jiaye Lin,Jianbo Lin,Siyu Zhang,Cheng Yang,Junxin Li,Yujia Li,Yu Huo,Ruixuan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大语言模型在代码推理中存在一种名为“酝酿”的内在机制，即答案在解码前已在内部表征中形成。通过双重诊断框架，研究发现传统准确率掩盖了四种深层失效模式，并指出尽管“酝酿”机制在模型间具有普遍性，但最终的推理成功率仍受限于模型的能力与规模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的标准准确率指标无法解释为什么大语言模型在处理变长跟踪等任务时表现良好，但在逻辑语义等价的循环任务中却会失败。研究旨在揭示模型在代码推理过程中的深层内部机制，通过识别模型在得出结论前经历的“酝酿”和“解析”阶段，探讨不同失效模式的成因，从而弥补表面评估的局限性。

Method: 作者提出了一套双重诊断框架：1. 层级线性探测（Layer-wise Linear Probing）：用于检测模型内部表示中答案的线性可恢复性；2. 去背景解码（Context-Stripped Decoding, CSD）：用于评估模型在没有上下文干扰下的推理能力。通过在16个大语言模型和6类代码推理任务上进行实验，并配合结构、深度和算子等变量的控制实验进行分析。

Result: 实验表明，大语言模型的代码推理遵循一种稳定的“酝酿”生命周期（约占推理过程的24-42%）。解析结果被归纳为四种模式：已解决（Resolved）、过度处理（Overprocessed）、误解（Misresolved）和未解决（Unresolved）。总体“已解决”率仅为41.5%，且随着任务难度（如函数调用深度）增加，性能急剧下降。研究证明，尽管推理的“酝酿”架构在不同模型中具有稳健性，但具体的解析成功率随模型能力和规模的变化呈现显著差异。

Conclusion: 研究发现，大语言模型在代码推理中存在一种稳定的“酝酿（brewing）”机制，即答案在被解码输出前早已在内部表征中形成。然而，模型最终能否正确输出答案（Resolution）则高度依赖于模型的能力、规模及训练，而非这种内在的推理结构。这一发现揭示了传统指标掩盖了模型在处理复杂任务时多样化的失效模式。

Abstract: Standard accuracy metrics cannot explain why LLMs handle variable tracking but fail on semantically equivalent loops. We study an internal lifecycle of code reasoning in which models first brew the answer, making it linearly recoverable many layers before it becomes self-decodable, and then diverge into one of four resolution outcomes: Resolved, Overprocessed, Misresolved, or Unresolved. Understanding this lifecycle matters because similar task accuracies can mask fundamentally different failure modes that surface-level evaluation cannot detect. We introduce a dual diagnostic framework pairing layer-wise linear probing with Context-Stripped Decoding (CSD) and apply it to six code-reasoning task families across 16 models spanning Qwen, Llama, and DeepSeek architectures. All four outcomes carry substantial mass in every task family: overall Resolved is only 41.5%, with multiple tasks below 30%. Controlled sweeps over structure, depth, and operators expose task-specific failure bottlenecks: Function Call Resolved plunges from 61.1% to 2.5% as call depth increases from one to three. Across architectures and scales, the brewing scaffold remains stable, with normalized brewing duration 24-42% across all 16 models, while resolution success varies with capability. This indicates that the scaffold is a stable empirical regularity across the tested decoder-only Transformer families, whereas resolution success covaries with capability, scale, and training. Code: https://github.com/euyis1019/llm-brewing

</details>


### [179] [Using Cognitive Models to Improve Language Model Simulation of Human Persuasion Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17657)
*Zirui Cheng,Zeyu Shen,Thomas L. Griffiths,Peter Henderson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出利用数学决策模型通过提示工程和强化学习来模拟人类多样的认知偏差，从而提升大语言模型在行为模拟、安全评估及训练场景中的真实性与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的模拟人类行为通常无法涵盖人类决策中复杂且多样化的认知偏见（如动机推理），导致其在安全评估和模型训练中存在局限性。研究旨在利用认知科学与经济学中的数学模型，使大语言模型能够更精准地模拟不同类型的人类决策行为。

Method: 提出了一种“公式到行为”（Equation-to-Behavior）的方法，包括两种具体路径：1. 通过提示工程（Prompting）引导大模型模拟贝叶斯更新、仿射失真、动机推理及Grether的α-β模型等决策过程；2. 通过强化学习（RL）训练小模型以遵循特定的决策数学规则。

Result: 实验表明，大模型可通过提示成功模拟多种数学决策模型，而小模型在强化学习训练后，在分布外参数化下的信念误差降低了26.5%。此外，通过引入多样化的决策者模型进行训练，模型在劝说任务中的表现提升了2.5%至12%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了利用数学模型（即“公式到行为”的方法）来引导大语言模型模拟人类多样化的决策行为是切实可行的。这不仅为大模型的安全评估和训练提供了更具广度和真实性的模拟环境，还为将行为科学引入人工智能研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: People make decisions differently in strategic interactions. Some update beliefs like a Bayesian; others exhibit biases like motivated reasoning. Although creators of large language models use simulated humans for safety evaluations and training, they often fail to cover this breadth of human behavior. We argue that cognitive science and economics provide a convenient tool for doing so, making use of mathematical models of human decision-making. We propose an approach that we call Equation-to-Behavior Prompting for guiding large language models to match cognitive models, and evaluate this approach on persuasion games based on legal decision-making. We find that large models can approximate equation-based specifications -- Bayesian updating, affine distortion, motivated updating, and Grether's $α$-$β$ model -- using prompting, but small models fail to do so. However, training small models with reinforcement learning to adhere to mathematical rules, Equation-to-Behavior RL, reduces belief error by 26.5% in out-of-distribution parameterizations. We show that these simulations can help create diverse training environments; training small models to consider different kinds of decision-makers improves average belief change by 2.5%--12% over Bayesian-only training, even when persuading GPT-5-mini. Our work could improve human simulations for training and evaluation in increasingly realistic settings, and could also enable novel research into more complicated mathematical models of human decision-making.

### [180] [FllumaOne: A Code-Native Multimodal CAD Dataset with Executable Programs and Kernel-Validated Feature Histories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17696)
*Jizong Zhan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FllumaOne是一个包含10万个高质量样本的代码原生多模态CAD数据集，通过将参数化建模过程与几何数据对齐，支持可编辑CAD的生成、逆向工程及多种下游任务，并提供了高精度的模型基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的CAD数据集往往缺乏对参数化建模过程（构造历史、操作序列、参数依赖）的完整记录。为了推动可编辑CAD技术的发展，需要一种能够同时暴露建模操作、参数依赖及几何验证结果的、代码原生的多模态数据集。

Method: 构建了基于Python代码执行的CAD数据集FllumaOne。该系统利用Flluma（基于Qt/C++和OpenCASCADE）生成模型，将代码、结构化特征树、STEP几何数据、点云、自然语言描述及渲染图等多模态信息进行对齐。通过严格的几何有效性和一致性校验，确保了数据的高质量。并在数据集上训练了Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B LoRA基准模型进行验证。

Result: 发布了FllumaOne-100K数据集，包含10万个高质量样本。基于Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B的实验显示，模型在代码语法有效性上达到99.98%，Flluma构建成功率达到99.97%，STEP导出有效性达到99.14%，在点云重构任务上表现优异，平均归一化Chamfer距离仅为0.002124。

Conclusion: FllumaOne为可编辑CAD研究提供了大规模、高质量、多模态的数据基准，有效连接了设计意图（代码/语言）与最终几何形态，为CAD生成式建模和自动化设计任务奠定了基础。

Abstract: Parametric computer-aided design records both final geometry and the ordered construction history that determines how a part can be edited. Datasets for editable CAD research should therefore expose modeling operations, parameters, and feature dependencies together with validated geometry. We introduce FllumaOne, a code-native multimodal CAD dataset whose models are generated by executable Python programs in Flluma, a Qt/C++ OpenCASCADE-based CAD system. Each sample aligns its program with a structured feature tree, a training-oriented intermediate representation, STEP geometry, a surface point cloud, natural-language descriptions, metadata, and eight canonical visible-edge renderings.
  The primary release, FllumaOne-100K, contains 100,000 accepted samples across four template-level complexity regimes. Programs are executed and retained only after kernel geometry, solid validity, and export checks; release reports also record modality completeness and split-level duplicate tests. A Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B LoRA baseline trained on 80,000 samples achieves 99.98% Python syntax validity, 99.97% Flluma build success, and 99.14% STEP-export validity on the held-out 10,000-sample test split. For the 9,909 predictions converted to surface point clouds, the mean normalized Chamfer Distance is 0.002124. The dataset supports conditioned CAD reconstruction, executable program synthesis, feature-tree prediction, B-Rep analysis, retrieval, design completion, and editable reverse engineering.

*Zeyao Du,Tong Li,Haibo Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 EComAgentBench，这是一个用于评估电商购物代理的新基准，通过将需求分散在不同交互阶段来模拟真实购物场景，并提供细粒度的失败归因分析，揭示了当前大模型在长流程购物决策中的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的购物代理评估基准过于简化，未能覆盖现实中用户需求呈现的多样性（如隐性需求、资料库记录或需要对话确认的需求），且无法解释模型失败的原因，导致现有评估难以反映代理在长流程交互中的真实表现。

Method: 构建了包含 662 个任务的 EComAgentBench 基准，任务需求分散在显式查询、受限的用户配置文件和交互式澄清中；引入了带有源标签的类型化评分方案，能够精确归因失败原因，并实现了自动化的基准构建流程。

Result: 对七种主流模型进行了评估，结果显示即使是表现最好的模型也仅达到 57.1% 的总体准确率；模型在处理从显式到隐性需求的信息提取能力上呈现显著下降趋势。

Abstract: As LLM-based shopping agents enter production, existing benchmarks fail to capture how a shopper's requirements arrive: stated implicitly in the query, recorded in a profile, or revealed only when the right question is asked. Benchmarks that expose full intent upfront and grade only the final choice can neither pose this long-horizon challenge nor explain which requirement an agent missed. To address this gap, we introduce EComAgentBench, a benchmark of 662 tasks grounded in real Amazon products and reviews. Each task scatters these requirements across a visible query, a tool-gated profile, and scripted clarification; an agent must uncover hidden intent, verify candidates against attributes and review evidence, and commit to a single product within 100 tool calls. Moreover, typed, source-tagged rubrics grade every task, attributing each failure to a requirement and its source. Construction is automated yet reliable, with every answer fixed in code before any text is generated and every sample validated. Our evaluation of seven models reveals that even the strongest attains only 57.1% overall accuracy, and rubric satisfaction degrades from visible to hidden sources. Overall, we believe EComAgentBench will serve as a reproducible foundation for moving shopping agents from single-query search toward dependable assistance over long horizons.

We further examine the automatic evaluation protocols through human agreement analysis. Experiments with state-of-the-art open-source and proprietary VLMs under single-image and multi-image settings reveal that structural fidelity degrades as webpage length increases, while visually plausible generations often fail to support executable multi-step interactions. These results highlight the need to evaluate long webpage generation beyond visual similarity, with executable interaction as a core criterion. ### [183] [Shattering the Autoregressive Curse: Dynamic Epistemic Entropy Orchestrated Erasable Reinforcement Learning for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17735)
*Ziliang Wang,Kang An,Faqiang Qian,Jialu Cai,Cijun Ouyang,Yuhang Wang,Qibing Ren,Yichao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对大模型在长链条逻辑推理中易产生“级联错误”的问题，提出了E3RL方法，通过利用模型内在不确定性实现逻辑错误的局部修剪与自我修复，大幅提升了模型在复杂数学推理任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在长序列逻辑推理中存在“自回归诅咒”问题，即早期生成的微小认知扰动会在马尔可夫决策过程中不断累积放大，导致级联失败，使得推理轨迹最终崩塌。现有方法难以解决这种单点错误导致后续推理全盘失效的问题。

Method: 提出动态认知熵编排的可擦除强化学习（E3RL）。该方法利用模型内生的局部交叉熵作为认知不确定性的指标，通过引入分段自适应阈值和优势分配机制，实现对局部逻辑缺陷的精准识别与修剪，并结合KV缓存流重用技术，赋予模型逻辑推理的自我修复能力。

Result: 在DeepMath-103k数据集上进行训练，实验表明E3RL显著提升了长序列推理的探索效率与样本效率，同时保持线性内存开销。在AIME等数学推理基准测试中，4B和8B模型性能分别提升了5.349%和6.514%，均超越了当时的先进水平（SOTA）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的E3RL框架通过引入自我修复机制，成功克服了长期逻辑推理中的“自回归诅咒”，证明了利用模型内在不确定性进行推理引导是提升大语言模型逻辑推理能力的有效路径，为迈向具备自愈能力的通用人工智能奠定了理论与系统基础。

Abstract: Although reinforcement learning (RL) has expanded the cognitive boundaries of large language models (LLMs), it often remains vulnerable to the autoregressive curse in long-horizon logical reasoning: small epistemic perturbations introduced early in generation can propagate irreversibly along the Markov decision process flow, triggering cascading failures that drive the reasoning trajectory toward collapse. To overcome this autoregressive cascade, in which a single early mistake can compromise all subsequent reasoning steps, we propose dynamic epistemic entropy orchestrated erasable reinforcement learning ($\text{E}^3\text{RL}$). $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ eliminates reliance on external signals by grounding the model's endogenous local autoregressive cross-entropy as an intrinsic coordinate of epistemic uncertainty. By introducing segment-level adaptive dynamic thresholds and advantage allocation, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ enables the model to precisely excise localized logical defects while reusing historical key-value (KV) cache streams, thereby endowing the reasoning process with a self-healing capability. We train $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ on the DeepMath-103k dataset. Experimental results show that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ reshapes the exploration efficiency of long-sequence reasoning and improves sample efficiency while maintaining linear memory overhead. On mathematical reasoning benchmarks such as AIME, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ achieves substantial performance gains, with the 4B and 8B parameter models surpassing previous state-of-the-art (SOTA) results by 5.349\% and 6.514\%, respectively. These findings suggest that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ shatters the autoregressive curse in long-sequence reasoning and establishes a theoretical and systems-level foundation for the next generation of self-healing artificial general intelligence (AGI).

### [184] [DecoSearch: Complexity-Aware Routing and Plan-Level Repair for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17821)
*Esteban Schafir,Xu Zheng,Hojat Allah Salehi,Zhuomin Chen,Mo Sha,Wei Cheng,Dongsheng Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecoSearch 是一个无需训练的 Text-to-SQL 框架，通过智能路由机制动态选择推理路径（直连或分解），结合模式裁剪和拓扑反馈优化，在大幅降低 token 开销的同时显著提升了复杂 SQL 生成的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在处理复杂、需要多步推理的 Text-to-SQL 任务时表现不佳，且现有的解决方法往往伴随着高额的计算开销或需要重新训练模型。旨在实现一种高效、无需训练的框架，根据查询复杂程度动态分配计算资源。

Method: 提出 DecoSearch 框架，包含三个核心模块：1. Schema Selector（轻量级模式裁剪）；2. LLM Judger（动态判断查询难度，决定是否采用 DAG 分解推理）；3. 拓扑精炼器（Topology Refiner，根据执行反馈调整推理路径）。此外整合了 RAG 技术进行上下文示例增强。

Result: DecoSearch 在 BIRD 数据集上达到了 70.53% 的执行准确率，在 Spider 上达到 88.31%，显著优于同类无需训练的基准方法，同时 token 消耗量降低了一个数量级。该方法具有通用性，可作为插件提升已微调模型的性能。

Conclusion: DecoSearch 证明了通过动态规划推理复杂度和优化上下文检索，无需额外训练即可显著提升 LLM 在 Text-to-SQL 任务中的性能。该框架证明了推理路径的灵活性（直连 vs. 分解）和纠错机制（拓扑精炼）是解决复杂数据库查询的关键。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in translating natural language to SQL, yet existing methods still falter on complex queries requiring multi-step, data-aware reasoning. We introduce DecoSearch, a training-free framework that addresses this by routing each query to the appropriate level of reasoning effort. A lightweight Schema Selector first prunes the full database schema to the relevant tables and columns. An LLM Judger then decides whether the question requires decomposition: straightforward questions follow a direct generation path and complex ones are escalated to a Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) of atomic sub-questions, each solved by a targeted SQL generation step. A RAG component grounds the decomposer with semantically similar training examples, and a Topology Refiner restructures the reasoning plan when execution failures signal a flawed decomposition rather than a fixable SQL error. DecoSearch achieves 70.53% execution accuracy on BIRD and 88.31% on Spider with a DeepSeek backbone, surpassing all training-free baselines while consuming an order of magnitude fewer tokens than competing methods. It also functions as a model-agnostic wrapper, consistently improving fine-tuned SQL generation backbones without any modification to the pipeline.

### [186] [A homotopy-type-theoretic generalization of neurosymbolic inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17851)
*Fernando Zhapa-Camacho,Robert Hoehndorf*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入同伦类型论，改进了神经符号系统的逻辑推理框架。通过显式建模对称性，作者证明了可以通过计算对称不变点来消除推理捷径，实现比集成学习更高效、更校准的推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的神经符号系统（如加权模型计数、模糊逻辑等）基于集合论，忽略了理论中的对称性和证明的多样性，导致模型容易产生“推理捷径”（推理偏差）。作者旨在引入同伦类型论，通过显式建模对称性来解决这一问题。

Method: 研究将神经符号系统基础由集合论替换为同伦类型论（HoTT），利用“同伦基数（homotopy cardinality）”来量化逻辑结构，使得系统能够捕捉并自动处理对称性。具体而言，该方法将推理捷径问题转化为混乱集单纯形上的对称不变点计算，并通过在对称群上平均单一模型来闭式计算概念后验。

Result: 在MNIST推理捷径基准测试中，该方法提出的单一模型封装器在保持标签准确性和概念可识别性的同时，相比多样性训练的集成模型，展现出更好的模型校准效果。

Conclusion: 该研究通过同伦类型论重构了神经符号系统的理论基础，提出了一种考虑对称性的推理框架。结论表明，利用对称性不变性可以在无需集成学习的情况下，仅通过单一模型推理即可有效解决推理捷径（reasoning shortcuts）问题，并在校准性上优于传统的集成方法。

Abstract: A wide range of neurosymbolic (NeSy) systems compute one functional: a belief-weighted sum of a logical quantity over a space of $σ$-structures, of which weighted model counting, fuzzy logic, and probabilistic logic are special cases. This account is built on sets, and a set deliberately forgets two things that are important for NeSy: when two $σ$-structures are the same up to a symmetry of the theory, and how many distinct proofs witness a query. Replacing the underlying sets by types, in the sense of homotopy type theory, preserves this information, and turns this functional into a belief-weighted homotopy cardinality, a notion of size that counts each object in inverse proportion to its symmetries. We develop the framework from scratch for NeSy systems, prove a conservativity theorem that recovers the classical functional when symmetries are trivial, and show that the symmetry our framework exposes is exactly the one behind reasoning shortcuts. The payoff is concrete: the shortcut-aware concept posterior that recent methods reach by ensembling or expressive density estimation is the only symmetry-invariant point of the confusion-set simplex, computable in closed form by averaging a single model over the symmetry group. On MNIST reasoning-shortcut benchmarks this single-model wrapper is better calibrated than a diversity-trained ensemble, while leaving label accuracy and identifiable concepts untouched. Code is freely available at https://github.com/bio-ontology-research-group/hott-nesy.

</details>


### [187] [FlowRAG: Synergizing Explicit Reasoning via Frequency-Aware Multi-Granularity Graph Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17856)
*Bihao Zhan,Zongsheng Cao,Jie Zhou,Bo Zhang,Liang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FlowRAG 是一种通过构建四层异构图并结合语义激活与频率加权路径规划的 GraphRAG 框架，显著改善了复杂多跳查询中的信息检索准确度与逻辑推理质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对现有基于实体的 GraphRAG 在处理抽象查询时召回不足，以及在多跳推理中易受噪声干扰导致推理链断裂的问题，旨在提升检索的语义感知能力与推理的可靠性。

Method: 1. 构建四层异构图（包含段落、摘要、句子和实体），利用摘要节点作为语义枢纽；2. 采用双粒度激活模块，结合摘要-查询对齐与句子级匹配以增强语义鲁棒性；3. 引入频率感知加权流模块，通过段落内词频加权实体-段落连接，剪枝噪声并提取高质量推理路径。

Result: FlowRAG 在多项复杂推理基准测试中达到了最先进的性能（SOTA），显著优于现有的各类检索增强生成方法。

Conclusion: FlowRAG 通过引入多层次语义图和基于频率的流式路由机制，有效提升了复杂查询任务中的语义召回率与推理路径的准确性，证明了显式语义结构在增强生成任务中的重要价值。

Abstract: Graph-based retrieval-augmented generation (GraphRAG) is effective for knowledge-intensive and multi-hop query tasks; however, many existing methods primarily seed entity-based graphs and rely on implicit semantic relevance propagation. This often (i) under-retrieves when user queries are abstract and semantically sparse at the entity level, and (ii) suffers from brittle multi-hop reasoning, where noisy activations can derail entity-to-entity transitions and corrupt the inferred relation chain, yielding unreliable conclusions. To this end, we propose \texttt{FlowRAG}, a semantic-aware retrieval framework that improves both semantic recall and explicit reasoning. Specifically, \texttt{FlowRAG} constructs a quad-level heterogeneous graph over passages, summaries, sentences, and entities, where summary nodes serve as a coarse semantic hub. At retrieval time, a dual-granularity activation module combines summary--query alignment with sentence-level matching to activate relevant entities under paraphrase and abstraction robustly. We then introduce a frequency-aware weighted flow module that routes relevance through entity--passage links weighted by within-passage term frequency, pruning noisy connections and extracting high-confidence reasoning paths as an explicit logic skeleton for generation. Extensive experiments show that \texttt{FlowRAG} obtains state-of-the-art performance on complex reasoning benchmarks.

### [188] [StepGuard: Guarding Web Navigation via Single-Step Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17871)
*Zhihao Cui,Yuchen Zhang,Xiyang Sun,Yaxiong Wang,Li Zhu,Jinpeng Hu,Liu Liu,Mengjia Li,Yujiao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: StepGuard 是一种新型 Web 导航框架，通过动态切换任务优先级与引入自适应反思机制，有效克服了传统智能体在网页操作中的奖励冲突与错误累积问题，大幅提升了导航与问答的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对当前 Web 导航智能体在执行任务时，因奖励错位导致的目标模糊以及因单步错误传播导致的整体性能下降（即单步脆弱性）问题，旨在构建一种能够自我校准并稳健执行任务的导航框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 StepGuard 的框架，包含两个核心模块：1. 动态双策略优化 (DDPO)：在导航优先和答案优先模式之间动态切换，缓解奖励冲突；2. 置信度引导的自适应导航反思 (CANR)：利用置信度评估触发反思，并通过对比奖励机制引导智能体进行自我修正。

Result: 实验结果表明，StepGuard 在主流 Web 导航基准测试中均设定了新的最先进 (SOTA) 水平，显著提高了导航成功率和问答准确率。

Conclusion: StepGuard 通过结合动态双策略优化和置信度引导的自适应导航反思机制，有效解决了 Web 导航任务中奖励错位和单步错误累积的问题，为提升自主智能体在复杂网页环境中的导航与问答准确性提供了稳健的方案。

Abstract: Web navigation requires agents to follow natural language goals, interact with web pages, and produce accurate answers. While recent advances leverage vision-language models and reinforcement learning, existing methods still suffer from single-step fragility due to reward misalignment and error propagation. To tackle the reward entanglement, we design Dynamic Dual-Policy Optimization (DDPO), which dynamically switches between a navigation-first mode for exploration and an answer-first mode for question-answering to mitigate reward conflict. To calibrate the single-step error, we propose Confidence-Guided Adaptive Navigation Reflection (CANR), a mechanism that estimates per-step confidence, triggers reflection only when necessary, and uses contrastive rewards to encourage self-correction to calibrate the single-step inaccuracy. With the above as the main components, we finally develop our StepGuard, a new framework of Guarding Web Navigation via Single-Step Calibration. Experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly improves navigation and answer accuracy, setting new state-of-the-art performance on standard web navigation benchmarks.

### [189] [Structural Preservation and the Logical Expressiveness of Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17882)
*Przemysław Andrzej Wałęga,Bernardo Cuenca Grau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过语义分析揭示了图神经网络（GNN）与分级模态逻辑之间的深层联系，证明了GNN在不同结构保持属性下的表达能力对应于特定的逻辑片段，且与具体架构选择无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GNN与逻辑形式之间的联系大多依赖于特定的架构选择（如聚合、组合和激活函数），这种方式限制了对GNN逻辑表达能力的理解。本文旨在超越具体的架构细节，通过语义视角探索GNN在结构保持特性下更广泛的逻辑表达能力。

Method: 本文采用了一种基于语义的方法，将GNN的分类器视为在特定结构属性（嵌入、单射同态、同态）下保持不变的类。通过利用有界高度树的良拟序（well-quasi-order）新结果，为这些不变类提供了有限表示，并证明了它们与分级模态逻辑及其子集（存在分级模态逻辑、存在正分级模态逻辑、存在正模态逻辑）的等价性。

Result: 研究表明：在嵌入保持下，GNN等价于存在分级模态逻辑；在单射同态保持下，等价于存在正分级模态逻辑；在同态保持下，等价于存在正模态逻辑。此外，作者证明了每一类逻辑特征都存在相应的GNN架构，验证了该理论框架的普适性。

Conclusion: 本文通过语义视角揭示了图神经网络（GNN）的逻辑表达能力，证明了GNN的结构保持特性与分级模态逻辑片段之间存在精确的对应关系。这一发现表明，GNN的表达能力并非完全依赖于特定的架构选择，而是植根于其固有的逻辑结构属性。

Abstract: Bridges between graph neural networks (GNNs) and logical formalisms have been established by fixing architectural choices, such as the types of aggregation, combination, and activation functions. These choices define restricted classes of GNNs for which tight correspondences with logical formalisms can be obtained, by showing that logical formulae can be translated into equivalent GNNs and, conversely, that GNNs can be translated into equivalent formulae.
  In this paper we take a semantic perspective by establishing the logical expressiveness of classes of GNN classifiers that are preserved under structural properties: embeddings (extensions), injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms. We show that, for each such property, there exists a fragment of graded modal logic characterising the class of GNNs. In particular, preservation under embeddings, injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms corresponds to existential graded modal logic, its existential-positive fragment, and existential-positive modal logic, respectively. These results characterise the expressiveness of broad classes of GNNs independently of specific architectural choices, but we also show that each of these classes admits a GNN architecture of the same expressiveness.
  Technically, our approach uses a new well-quasi-order result for trees of bounded height, yielding finite representations of unravelling-invariant classes.

This gives rise to two core issues: first, the supervisory signals for visual content are generalized and coarse-grained, lacking adaptation to the actual necessity of visual information in each sample; second, training feedback becomes inaccurate when visual rewards are uniformly applied without distinguishing the complementary relationships among inputs. These limitations hinder models from achieving precise multimodal reasoning. In this work, we propose a framework for modeling fine-grained visual dependencies in mathematical reasoning. We first construct the MathVis-Fine dataset, augmenting fine-grained visual annotations with visual dependency ratings. Building upon this dataset, we introduce a two-stage progressive visual enhancement training paradigm that balances answer correctness rewards and visual grounding rewards according to the intrinsic visual dependency level of each sample, thereby mitigating reward bias and improving supervision accuracy. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the MathVis-Fine framework effectively enhances visual perception progressively based on visual dependency, offering a more precise training framework for multimodal mathematical reasoning. Learn to cluster is label-free and can be naturally integrated into the training process of the prediction model. The latent variables will then serve as 'labels' to categorize social interactions. Extensive experiments over several trajectory prediction benchmarks demonstrate that our method is able to learn the patterns of social interactions and effectively integrate the patterns to pedestrian trajectory prediction.

### [192] [DiagFlowBench: Evaluating How Language Models Handle Off-Procedure Inputs in Grounded Diagnostic Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17904)
*Guillermo Gil de Avalle,Laura Maruster,Shaina Raza,Christos Emmanouilidis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了DiagFlowBench基准测试，用于评估工业大模型处理“超出范围”用户查询的能力，发现当前模型在面对非预期输入时，极易因从文档中盲目提取看似合理但实际错误的建议而导致误导，而非单纯的幻觉式捏造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型在工业维护中被用作咨询系统，但为了防止幻觉而采用的“文档接地（grounding）”技术往往无法应对用户偏离预定流程的提问。现有的基准测试缺乏对模型识别“超出范围（out-of-scope）”输入能力的评估，因此需要新的工具来测试模型在复杂工业场景下的鲁棒性。

Method: 研究者构建了DiagFlowBench数据集，包含50个工业诊断流程图，并将其转化为1,676个多轮对话。这些对话特别设计了合规请求与超出范围请求的对比，用于评估十种商业及开源模型在处理非预期输入时的表现。

Result: 评估结果显示，各模型在识别并拒绝回答超出范围问题（即“弃权”）的能力上差异巨大。研究发现，模型在面对不明确的请求时，更倾向于从文档中选择一个虽然真实存在但上下文中不适用的步骤进行错误建议，而不是直接生成捏造的事实，这种隐蔽的错误模式更具误导性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了现有大模型在工业维护场景中，即使在有文档引导的情况下，也容易提供“虽合理但错误”的建议。这种倾向于选择上下文中不当步骤而非直接虚构事实的特性，构成了一种极具挑战性的安全脆弱性，强调了模型在识别“范围外（out-of-scope）”问题上能力提升的紧迫性。

Abstract: Language models increasingly serve as advisory systems in maintenance operations. To prevent hallucination, recent systems ground these models in procedural documentation to constrain them to approved steps. In practice, however, operator queries frequently stray from this path, requiring models to recognise out-of-scope inputs mid-conversation, a dynamic that current benchmarks rarely prioritise. We introduce DiagFlowBench, a dataset of 50 industrial diagnostic flowcharts from a consumer manufacturer converted into 1,676 multi-turn conversations that contrast compliant with out-of-scope utterances. Evaluating a panel of ten commercial and open-weight models reveals high variability in abstention rates, with models commonly selecting a real but contextually inadequate step rather than fabricating facts. The inherent plausibility and authority of this mapped but wrong advice exposes a challenging vulnerability for grounding systems.

### [193] [PreAct: Computer-Using Agents that Get Faster on Repeated Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17929)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PreAct 是一种通过将成功任务编译为轻量级状态机并进行验证性重用来加速计算机自动化 Agent 的方法，在不牺牲准确性的前提下，将重复任务的执行效率提升了 8.5-13 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的计算机自动化 Agent 在重复执行已知任务时，往往需要重新推理、重新进行视觉处理并调用语言模型，导致了极高的计算成本和响应延迟。作者旨在提出一种机制，使 Agent 能够从既往经验中学习，通过重用之前的执行路径来加速任务执行，同时保证执行的可靠性。

Method: PreAct 方法：1. 任务编译：当 Agent 成功完成任务后，将其操作序列编译成轻量级状态机（包含状态检查和动作转换）；2. 执行回放：后续执行时直接运行状态机，跳过语言模型调用，实现快速响应；3. 执行验证：在每一步执行前检查屏幕状态，若不匹配则回退至 Agent 控制；4. 存储校验：仅存储经独立评估器验证确实成功的程序，避免无效程序的积累。

Result: 1. 效率提升：在重复任务中，速度比传统 Agent 提升了 8.5 到 13 倍；2. 准确性保证：通过存储前的独立评估和运行时的动态监控，有效过滤了故障程序；3. 广泛适用性：在移动端、桌面端和 Web 基准测试中均表现一致，显著优于传统的简单回放基准线。

Conclusion: PreAct 通过将复杂的 Agent 任务转化为轻量级的状态机程序，有效地解决了 Agent 重复执行任务时的高延迟和高成本问题。该方法不仅在效率上实现了显著提升，还通过严格的验证机制确保了任务执行的准确性和鲁棒性，为提升自动化 Agent 的长期实用性提供了一种高效的策略。

Abstract: Computer-using agents drive real software through the screen -- clicking and typing -- but they solve every task from scratch: asked to repeat a task, an agent re-reads the screen, re-reasons every tap, and pays the full cost again. We present PreAct, which lets such an agent get faster on tasks it has done before. The first time it succeeds, PreAct compiles the run into a small state-machine program-states that check the screen, transitions that act-and on later runs replays it directly instead of invoking the agent 8.5-13x faster, with no per-step language-model calls. Replay is not blind: at each step PreAct checks that the screen matches what the program expects before acting, and hands control back to the agent the moment something is off.
  PreAct applies the same discipline when deciding what to keep: a freshly compiled program enters the store only if, re-run from a clean state, an independent evaluator confirms it solved the task-catching programs that replay to their last step yet leave the task undone. Across a mobile, a desktop, and a web benchmark, this store-time check separates repeated runs that improve from ones that degrade as faulty programs accumulate, worth 1.75-2.6 tasks per benchmark, the same direction on all three; a fallback that explores afresh when no program fits brings PreAct level with a strong record-and-replay baseline. We also report what did not matter: prompt wording, runtime guardrails, and whether a language model or a plain embedding retriever selects which program to reuse.

</details>


### [194] [How Inference Compute Shapes Frontier LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17930)
*Jessica McFadyen,Ole Jorgensen,Harry Coppock,Kevin Wei,Cozmin Ududec*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出AI模型性能与推理时算力分配紧密相关，单一的固定预算评估会导致对模型真实能力的低估，建议采用基于推理算力函数的动态评估协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI评估正转向更复杂的任务，模型性能日益依赖于推理时的算力分配。然而，现有的评估通常在单一、受限的预算下进行，导致测试结果往往反映的是评估配置而非模型真实能力，从而低估了先进模型的能力。

Method: 研究人员在软件工程、数学、医学和网络安全等领域的七个挑战性基准测试上评估了最多12个前沿语言模型。采用受控实验方法，结合了三种推理算力扩展干预手段：增加Token预算、上下文压缩以及基于模型自反馈或最小正确性反馈的重复提交策略。

Result: 1. 增加Token预算能显著提升跨多个领域（如网络安全、数学等）的性能；2. 随着模型进化，固定预算评估会越来越低估前沿能力，高性能模型在更大预算下能解锁并解决更难的任务；3. 不同基准测试对各种推理扩展方法的敏感度不同，重复提交具有通用提升效果，但其他方法的有效性因任务而异。

Conclusion: 基准测试分数高度依赖于评估协议。本文主张未来的模型评估应将能力描述为推理时算力的函数，明确指定协议选择，并在大规模共享算力范围内进行跨代比较，特别是在涉及安全和政策的评估中。

Abstract: AI evaluations are shifting toward harder tasks that benefit from longer trajectories involving tool use and iterative problem solving. As a result, performance is increasingly sensitive to the amount and allocation of compute available at test time ("inference compute"). Yet many evaluations still report performance at a single restrictive budget, meaning that low scores may reflect the evaluation setup rather than the model's underlying capability. To test this, we evaluate up to 12 frontier language models on seven challenging benchmarks spanning software engineering, mathematics, medicine, and cybersecurity. We use a controlled setup combining three simple inference-scaling interventions: larger token budgets, context compaction, and repeated submission attempts, guided either by the model itself or by minimal correctness feedback. We find three main results. First, larger token budgets substantially improve performance on benchmarks across multiple domains, including cybersecurity, FrontierMath, Humanity's Last Exam, and TerminalBench. Second, fixed-budget evaluations can increasingly understate frontier capability as models advance. Newer models reach higher performance at large budgets, where they unlock harder tasks and solve them more reliably. Third, benchmarks differ in which inference-scaling methods help most: repeated submission broadly improves performance, but the value of larger token budgets, external feedback, and parallel attempts varies by benchmark. Overall, our results show that benchmark scores are protocol-dependent. We therefore argue that evaluations should report capability as a function of inference-time compute, specify protocol choices explicitly, and compare model generations over a large shared compute range at matched budgets, especially in safety- or policy-relevant settings.

</details>


### [195] [Small Initialization Matters for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17945)
*Liangkai Hang,Junjie Yao,Zhiyu Li,Feiyu Xiong,Hongkang Yang,Zhi-Qin John Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究揭示了参数初始化规模是影响大模型推理能力的关键因素，提出了一种通过减小初始化规模来优化模型训练轨迹、增强推理性能的通用规则（γ-初始化）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型研究多关注规模、数据和架构对智能的影响，但参数初始化作为决定训练过程和模型能力的基础因素，其重要性尚未得到充分探讨。本文旨在揭示参数初始化如何作为一种“基因”影响模型的容量与推理能力。

Method: 本文通过实证研究探讨了参数初始化规模对大模型性能的影响；识别并排除了限制小初始化优势的两个传统经验设置；通过机制分析（包括参数结构的演变和Token级预测分析）验证了较小初始化带来的训练轨迹优化。

Result: 较小的初始化规模能够持续提升预训练效果，特别是在需要深度推理的任务上提升最为显著；小初始化引导模型参数经历从低复杂度结构向丰富表示的“凝练-扩张”过程，验证了“压缩即智能”的理念；该方法在几乎不增加成本的情况下提升了模型性能。

Conclusion: 参数初始化是决定大语言模型训练和模型能力的关键“基因”；提出了一种简单且低成本的“γ-初始化规则”，即默认使用较小的初始化规模，能够显著提升预训练效率并增强模型的推理能力。

Abstract: Large language models provide a tractable system for asking how intelligence itself emerges, rather than only how LLMs can be engineered. Although progress is usually attributed to scale, data and architecture, we show that parameter initialization is a gene-like determinant of training and, in particular, of model capacity. Reducing the initialization scale consistently improves pretraining, with the largest gains on reasoning-demanding tasks. We identify two widely used empirical settings that restrain the advantage of small initialization, and show how relaxing them restores favorable scaling. We further uncover a critical initialization that balances the reasoning and training. Mechanistically, small initialization drives a distinct developmental trajectory: parameters first condense into low-complexity structures and later expand into richer representations, giving concrete form to the idea that compression is intelligence. Token-level analyses show that the gains concentrate on non-trivial, context-constrained predictions rather than all tokens uniformly. These results motivate a simple $γ$-initialization rule: expose initialization rage as an explicit knob and use small initialization by default, an almost cost-free intervention that improves pretraining and strengthens reasoning across model scales.

</details>


### [196] [MoCo-AIS: A Contrastive Learning Framework for Similarity Computation of Vessel Trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17978)

Result: 实验结果表明，MoCo-AIS 框架显著优于现有的基线模型，能够更高效地进行轨迹相似度学习，并有效验证了不同深度学习模型在处理复杂船舶导航行为时的性能。

Abstract: Trajectory similarity is a fundamental task in analyzing mobility patterns, essential for applications such as route pattern extraction, mobility prediction, and anomaly detection. Traditional distance-based measures for computing similarity incur high computational cost, driving the adoption of lightweight learning-based approaches. Supervised methods rely on extensive labels derived from traditional distance measures and often reproduce these metrics, which limits generalization. While self-supervised learning addresses this issue through contrastive learning, it lacks a unified framework, making it difficult to compare deep learning (DL) models for consistent trajectory representation. Accordingly, this paper presents MoCo-AIS, a unified framework for learning vessel trajectory embeddings based on the Momentum Contrast (MoCo) paradigm, which formulates similarity learning through positive and negative trajectory pairs. Within this framework, we evaluate a diverse set of leading DL models on large-scale, real-world vessel-tracking AIS datasets that capture diverse navigation behaviors and operating conditions. Results demonstrate that our framework significantly improves similarity learning over existing baselines, while providing a benchmarking platform for evaluating trajectory representation models.

### [197] [STAR: SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward Allocation for Text-to-Image RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17979)
*Jinjie Shen,Wei Deng,Xian Hu,Daiguo Zhou,Jian Luan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: STAR 提出了一种针对扩散模型强化学习后训练的时空自适应奖励分配方案，通过将奖励更精准地分配给与生成内容高度相关的时空区域，大幅提升了图像生成的语义对齐与文本渲染效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本生成图像强化学习后训练方法通常将最终奖励处理为单一标量优势，并均匀作用于整个生成轨迹。然而，扩散模型生成图像具有明确的时空结构，且文本对齐往往只与图像的部分区域相关，这种颗粒度上的失配导致模型无法聚焦于真正影响奖励的关键生成组件。

Method: 提出了一种“时空自适应奖励（STAR）分配”方法。该方法利用生成模型内部的文本-图像注意力机制，识别用户提示词中的核心内容；通过构建随去噪步骤和采样过程动态变化的“空间分配图”，将优势值（advantage）更精准地分配给图像中与奖励最相关的潜空间区域，并对这些区域实施更强的策略更新。

Result: 在 Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium 基础上进行实验，STAR 在 GenEval、OCR 文本渲染和 PickScore 三项任务上分别取得了 0.9759、0.9757 和 23.60 的优秀成绩，证明了其在提升组合语义对齐能力、文本渲染精度及人类偏好优化方面的显著效果。

Conclusion: STAR 框架有效解决了文本生成图像过程中奖励分配不均的问题。通过引入时空自适应的策略优化，该方法在不改变外部奖励源的情况下，显著提升了生成模型在语义对齐、文本渲染及人类偏好等方面的表现，证明了针对生成轨迹进行精细化控制对于强化学习后训练的重要性。

Abstract: Existing RL post-training methods for text-to-image generation usually convert the final-image reward into a single scalar advantage and apply it with the same strength to the entire generative trajectory. However, text-to-image generation naturally has temporal and spatial structure: different denoising steps are responsible for different generation stages, and the content that truly determines text alignment often appears only in part of the image. This granularity mismatch makes it difficult for policy updates to focus on the generative components that actually affect the reward. To address this issue, we propose \textbf{SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward (STAR) Allocation} for RL post-training of text-to-image diffusion and flow models. STAR uses text-image attention inside the generative model and starts from the core content that the user truly cares about in the prompt. It constructs spatial allocation maps that dynamically vary across denoising steps and rollouts, and allocates the same group-relative advantage to more relevant latent regions with almost no additional computational overhead. STAR then applies stronger policy updates to these regions through a spatially resolved policy objective. We use Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium as the base model and evaluate on three tasks: GenEval, OCR text rendering, and PickScore. Experimental results show that STAR improves compositional semantic alignment, text rendering, and preference optimization without changing the external reward source, achieving $\mathbf{0.9759}$, $\mathbf{0.9757}$, and $\mathbf{23.60}$ on GenEval, OCR, and PickScore, respectively.

Conclusion: 本文通过界定“LLM消费者行为理论”这一新兴研究领域，为理解人工智能代理在市场中的作用提供了理论框架。文章强调，随着代理决策在消费领域变得普遍，传统的经济学假设（如完全理性）需要重新评估，以适应人机协作和代理驱动的复杂市场生态。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents that make consumption decisions on behalf of users. We unify previously fragmented literature on LLM decision-making, human behavior simulation, and preference elicitation under a common economic lens, highlighting where assumptions, such as rationality and heterogeneity, may fail in agentic markets. ### [199] [LegalHalluLens: Typed Hallucination Auditing and Calibrated Multi-Agent Debate for Trustworthy Legal AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18021)
*Lalit Yadav,Akshaj Gurugubelli*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对法律AI系统错误诊断模糊的问题，本文提出了 LegalHalluLens 框架。通过类型化分析和风险方向量化，揭示了聚合指标掩盖的性能短板，并利用针对性辩论机制有效降低了幻觉，实现了对法律AI风险的精细化评估与校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的法律AI系统在处理法律工作流时存在约52%的平均幻觉率，但这一聚合指标掩盖了错误分布的细微差别（如不同类型声明间的巨大性能差异及风险倾向），使得合规官难以评估模型在实际法律环境下的可信度和可靠性。

Method: 1. 提出 LegalHalluLens 审计框架，包含四类法律动机声明的类型化幻觉分析；2. 构建风险方向指数（RDI），用于量化遗漏与虚构偏差；3. 设计校准后的多智能体辩论管道（Debate Pipeline），针对性地修正特定类型的模型故障。

Conclusion: 现有的法律AI评估方法过度依赖聚合指标（如平均幻觉率），导致无法识别风险类型及方向。本文提出的 LegalHalluLens 框架通过类型化分析、风险方向指数（RDI）及针对性的多智能体辩论机制，为法律AI的部署提供了更具可操作性的诊断与校准工具，实现了更可信的法律AI系统构建。

Abstract: AI systems deployed in legal workflows hallucinate at rates that aggregate metrics report at ~52%, but this average conceals where errors concentrate and in which direction they run, leaving compliance officers without an actionable signal for trustworthy deployment. We present LegalHalluLens, an auditing framework with three components: typed hallucination profiles across four legally-motivated claim categories (numeric, temporal, obligation/entitlement, factual) over CUAD (Hendrycks et al., 2021); a Risk Direction Index (RDI) that reduces omission-versus-invention bias to a single deployment-comparable scalar; and a typed debate pipeline calibrated to both magnitudes and directions. Across 510 contracts and 249,252 clause-level instances we measure a within-model gap of approximately 38-40 pp between obligation/numeric and temporal claims that aggregate reporting hides, and show that two systems with matched 52% rates can carry opposite RDIs. The debate pipeline reduces fabricated detections by 45% with per-category gains tracking the diagnosis, matching commercial APIs with a substantially smaller backbone (4B active parameters). Typed profiles and RDI surface failure modes that aggregate metrics hide; we further show these diagnostics serve as calibration inputs for multi-agent debate pipelines, where Skeptic challenges and asymmetric gates targeted at measured failure modes outperform generically-tuned debate. The framework supports direction-aware procurement, accountability, and agent design for legal AI deployed in the wild.

### [200] [ProvenanceGuard: Source-Aware Factuality Verification for MCP-Based LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18037)
*Ander Alvarez,Santhiya Rajan,Samuel Mugel,Román Orús*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 智能体在多源数据调用中常见的“张冠李戴”式归因错误（跨源混淆），本文提出了 ProvenanceGuard 验证系统，通过追踪原子声明的证据来源，实现了对回答事实性和归因准确性的精准验证与修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的事实性指标主要关注回答是否由汇总证据支持，忽略了“跨源混淆”这一关键失败模式，即回答内容虽正确但归因于错误的证据源，这在医疗等高风险领域具有严重后果。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ProvenanceGuard 的来源感知验证器。该方法通过：1. 解析 MCP 跟踪记录以提取工具和源信息；2. 将回答分解为原子声明；3. 将声明路由至特定来源；4. 利用自然语言推理（NLI）和标记对齐代理检查证据支持度；5. 比对声明的归因与实际证据源；6. 若检测到错误，通过检索增强的回答修订机制进行修复和重验证。

Result: 在医疗领域 MCP 智能体跟踪数据集上的实验表明：在 40 个留出测试集上，ProvenanceGuard 实现了 0.802 的阻塞 F1 分数和 0.858 的来源准确率。在 50 个受控临床混淆探针中，该工具成功检测出所有注入的归因错误，并能通过修复机制有效消除错误归因。

Conclusion: 研究证明，来源归因是评估基于模型上下文协议（MCP）的智能体事实性的一个独立且关键的维度。ProvenanceGuard 有效解决了跨源混淆问题，显著提升了智能体回答的可靠性和可追溯性。

Abstract: Tool-using LLM agents increasingly use the Model Context Protocol (MCP) to answer from heterogeneous evidence sources, including search, APIs, databases, clinical records, and formulary tools. Standard factuality metrics usually test whether an answer is supported by pooled evidence, missing a provenance-sensitive failure mode: a claim may be supported somewhere while being attributed to the wrong source. We call this cross-source conflation.
  We introduce ProvenanceGuard, a source-aware verifier for MCP-grounded answers. It consumes captured MCP traces with stable tool IDs, source IDs, and raw outputs; decomposes answers into atomic claims; routes claims to source-specific evidence; checks support with NLI and a token-alignment proxy; compares stated attribution with the routed source; and returns per-claim verdicts plus an answer-level allow/block decision. Blocked answers can be repaired with retrieval-augmented answer revision and re-verified.
  We evaluate on 281 medical-domain MCP-agent traces. A 266-trace adjudicated subset yields 2,325 LLM-assisted claim labels split by trace; 361 held-out labels are human-verified. On the 40-trace held-out split, ProvenanceGuard achieves block F1 0.802 and source accuracy 0.858 over 260 source-eligible claims, outperforming source-blind baselines that do not emit claim-to-source IDs. On a harder multi-source benchmark it reaches block F1 0.846, while source-plus-relation accuracy drops to 0.229, showing that exact source ownership remains difficult with semantically close sources. Repair-and-reverify resolves all blocked answers in the full trace set, often via conservative fallback. In 50 controlled clinical conflation probes, ProvenanceGuard detects all injected attribution swaps with no retained wrong attribution. These results show that source attribution is an independent axis for factuality verification in MCP-based agents.

We present PseudoBench, an adversarial benchmark for evaluating whether agentic auto-research systems can identify and resist pseudoscientific narratives. PseudoBench contains 200 curated pseudoscientific claim-evidence pairs across five domains and evaluates agents through an end-to-end research pipeline from experiments to writing. Testing seven state-of-the-art agents, we find that current systems readily produce persuasive reports that align with pseudoscientific premises with near-zero refusal rates and the highest resistance of only 27.4%. Stronger agents risk packaging pseudoscience in more sophisticated scientific language, increasing its apparent credibility. These findings reveal an alarming capacity to fuel pseudoscience, calling for scientific alignment before widespread deployment.

In this work, we propose a multi-agent framework that addresses both issues by replacing ``LLM-as-a-judge'' routing with deterministic orchestration constraints. The framework incorporates two safety mechanisms. First, a neuro-symbolic state-tracking gate enforces completeness of the OLDCARTS clinical protocol (Onset, Location, Duration, Character, Aggravating/Alleviating factors, Radiation, Timing, and Severity) by blocking diagnostic transitions until all required dimensions are collected. Second, an epistemic uncertainty quantification (UQ) gate computes semantic entropy (H) across K=5 independent diagnostic samples to identify and intercept divergent outputs before delivery.
  We evaluate the system using simulated patient agents powered by the llama-3.1-70b-instruct model on 150 test cases. Additionally, we observe a statistically significant negative correlation (r = -0.181, p < 0.05) between OLDCARTS completeness (σ) and semantic entropy (H), suggesting that structured information gathering is associated with reduced diagnostic uncertainty.

### [203] [A Unified Framework for Context-Aware and Relation-Aware Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18075)
*Haoyang Zhong,Yifei Sun,Antong Zhang,Chunping Wang,Lei Chen,Yang Yang*

TL;DR: HyGRAG 是一种分层图 RAG 框架，通过混合图建模与层次化总结实现了真正的知识融合，显著提升了多跳推理能力并支持动态知识库更新。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于图的 RAG 方法存在局限性，即实体中心与文本块中心的方法均基于原始文本，缺乏深层的知识融合，导致在检索时难以挖掘出隐藏的关联理解和跨文档的演生知识。

Method: 提出 HyGRAG 框架，构建包含文本块与实体节点的混合分层图结构；通过迭代聚类与大模型总结实现知识融合；设计支持跨抽象层级且具备社区扩展能力的上下文与关系感知检索算法；并采用基于局部重总结的附着式算法实现动态知识更新。

Result: 实验结果表明，HyGRAG 在多跳推理任务中的平均准确率提升了 9.7%，并在保持合理的计算效率前提下实现了高效的知识更新。

Conclusion: HyGRAG 通过分层图结构和总结机制成功融合了上下文与实体关系，有效克服了传统检索增强生成（RAG）在知识融合上的局限，为多跳推理任务提供了更高效、更精准的解决方案。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has emerged as a paradigm for enhancing large language models (LLMs) with external knowledge, yet existing graph-based methods face a fundamental limitation: entity-centric and chunk-centric approaches operate on representations anchored to original text without true knowledge fusion. While entity-centric methods connect logically related content and chunk-centric methods preserve context, both retrieve information separately through similarity search, missing emergent understanding from their synthesis. In this paper, we propose HyGRAG, a hierarchical graph RAG framework that transcends source documents by addressing three core challenges: constructing summaries that genuinely integrate contextual and relational information, leveraging these synthesized representations to access emergent knowledge during retrieval, and efficiently updating hierarchical structures for dynamic corpora. Specifically, we design hierarchical index structures over hybrid graphs with both chunk and entity nodes, then iteratively cluster them and generate LLM-based summaries. Then, we design context and relation-aware retrieval that searches across all abstraction levels while expanding through community membership. Moreover, we enable dynamic knowledge update through attachment-based algorithms with only local re-summarization. Experimental results show that HyGRAG improves the average accuracy of multi-hop reasoning tasks by 9.7%, while maintaining reasonable efficiency.

</details>

Abstract: Advances in Artificial Intelligence (AI) have led AI for Theorem Proving to become a promising means of formally verifying computer systems. In this paper, we improve upon IsabeLLM, the automated theorem proving tool in Isabelle.
